Refining the elixir demands discerning effort—
Day and night, diligently tend the crucible.
When the first **Yáng** [阳, Yang] stirs,
Harvest it tender—let it wither when ripe.

When clouds disperse and rain ceases after the elixir congeals,
The zither and **sè** [瑟, se] harmonize in that moment.
Beware—do not rush the fire’s timing,
For ignorance of restraint invites peril."*

**Huányáng Zhēnrén** [还阳真人] says:
*"When the first **Yáng** [阳, Yang] stirs, there is no contrivance—
Yet contrivance disturbs the compass needle.
Obtain the **Niúmián** [牛眠, cow-sleep] **qi**-cavern,
Where the **mùlián** [墓莲, tomb lotus] blooms seven golden petals."*

**Chōngxū Zǐ** [冲虚子] says:
*"Where the first **Yáng** [阳, Yang] stirs is the **Xuānguān** [玄关, Mysterious Pass].
No need for doubt, no need for difficulty.
Now is the time to stand before the crucible, following the oral precepts—
The path will reveal itself naturally through the **níwán** [泥丸, mud pill].

When the first **Yáng** [阳, Yang] stirs, its ebb is slow—
This is the immortal’s hour for gathering.
Swiftly apply the function according to the oral precepts,
Lest you miss this moment."*

**Chóngyáng Zhēnrén** [重阳真人] says:
*"Beneath pure **Yīn** [阴, Yin], fire must first temper and forge,
Then **Yáng qi** [阳气, Yang vitality] arises—
The divine clarity comes naturally.
Divine clarity is the wondrous awakening of true essence and original **Yáng** [阳, Yang].
**Lóngméizǐ** [龙眉子] says: *'The **Fènglún** [凤轮, phoenix wheel] stirs, producing true lead.'*
The mechanism must first be primed,
Then the elixir is born to undergo the fire."*

*The **Màiyì** [脉益] says:*
*"The **Kūn** [坤, Receptive] vessel is originally empty.
At twenty-one years, touched by the father’s luminous essence,
**Yáng qi** [阳气, Yang vitality] begins to move—
The **Gāndǐng** [干鼎, dry crucible] holds nothing.
When gathering, absorb the **Kūnmǔ** [坤母, Receptive Mother]’s **Yáng** lead—
Then the **Jīndān** [金丹, golden elixir] begins to congeal.

The true mechanism lies within a fleeting instant,
Its marvel in the **yǎomíng** [窈冥, profound darkness].
The profound darkness’s true essence arises from emptiness—
Unseen, it defies observation.
Seize the moment when sun and moon align in harmony,
When the square and compass dissolve—
Guard it with utmost caution,
Seek it in silent stillness,
Only then may you command the elixir’s crucible
And perform the **yīfú èrhòu** [一符二候, one symbol and two signs] alchemy.
The slightest negligence rarely fails to ruin the work.

Preserve the **wú** [无, non-being], guard the **yǒu** [有, being],
Wait within the void—
This is the method of seeking lead,
Daring not the slightest deviation,
Thus attaining the **jīnqíng guīxìng** [金情归性, golden sentiment returning to nature],
And completing our transformative endeavor."*

**Níwán Zǔ** [泥丸祖] says:
*"When spirit and **qi** merge in obscurity and vitality returns,
Flesh and bone dissolve in unison—none perceive.
The **guānjié** [关节, passes and joints] open spontaneously, the hundred vessels flow,
Form and countenance radiate like an infant’s."*

*The **Zhōnghé Jí** [中和集] says:*
*"When **Tiānguǐ** [天癸, celestial water] first emerges,
True **Yáng** [阳, Yang] naturally responds.
The **Sānmèi** [三昧, threefold meditation] fire, though dwelling below, erupts upward—
A single sound resounds from the **Gōng** [宫, palace].
**Qi** and spirit harmonize, birthing sacred substance,
Heart and breath interdependent, forming the holy embryo.
Piercing the inner message,
The three passes and nine orifices open as one."*

*The **Tiānxiān Zhènglǐ** [天仙正理] says:*
*"**Qi** and spirit both have motion and stillness—
At the extreme of stillness, motion’s seed arises.
When **qi** moves, spirit moves—
The moment original **qi** stirs, the spirit’s wondrous awakening begins.
Gathering and refining occur at this most exquisite juncture."*

*The **Tiānxiān Zhènglǐ** [天仙正理] says:*
*"True **Yáng qi** [真阳之气, true Yang vitality] inherently lacks form.
The ancients spoke only of *'the **qi** of emptiness.'*
Its manifestation—
Formless adhering to form—
Permeates within and without, this **qi**’s flow.
In gathering, fire is borrowed for extraction—
No elixir’s shape is seen,
Only fire is known.
The ancient hymn says: *'Fire and elixir originally dwell as one—
When viewed, it seems present; when sought, it vanishes.'*
Again it says: *'Gather the elixir’s substance within the unmoving,
Apply the fire’s timing within the effortless.'*"*

*The **Tiānxiān Zhènglǐ** [天仙正理] says:*
*"The **Jiājí** [夹脊, spine’s junction] and **Wěilǘ** [尾闾, tail’s gate] hold the secret—
Truly so, this refers to prior elixir-gathering.
When essence and **qi** generate and move,
It is also the profound darkness returning to stillness,
Also the profound darkness’s fire and **qi** steeping for a hundred days—
Thus, true **qi** emerges, suddenly visible.
Therefore, halt the **Hòutiān** [后天, post-heavenly] **qi**’s fire,
And solely gather the **Xiāntiān** [先天, pre-heavenly] elixir’s **yào** [药, medicine].
Thus, another seven days’ work is employed,
Gathering within those seven days.
At this time, true **qi** fully returns to the **mìnggēn** [命根, root of life].
Though movement occurs, it does not cling to the place of motion,
Remaining within yet not dispersing outward.
Its use involves fire without fire,
Timing without timing—
This differs from before.
Here begins the great matter of nurturing spirit and returning to the void,
Here begins the attainment of longevity, transcending calamities, and communing with the **Wújí** [无极, ultimate extremity].
Thus it is named the **Dàyào** [大药, great medicine], also **Jīndān** [金丹, golden elixir]—
The reality attained from gathering the **qi** of emptiness."*

*The **Tiānxiān Zhènglǐ** [天仙正理] says:*
*"Our teachers employ seven days’ work,
And by the fifth day, the **Dāntián** [丹田, elixir field] glows like a fire-pearl.
It should rush upward to the heart,
Then descend toward the outer kidney’s edge—
No orifice for exit, it turns toward the **Wěilǘ** [尾闾, tail’s gate] and **Chōngguān** [冲关, piercing the pass].
These are the marvelous operations of true **qi** itself.
Yet at the pass’s edge,
Oral transmission of celestial mechanism is required
To traverse it."*

*The **Tiānxiān Zhènglǐ** [天仙正理] says:*
*"Consuming the **Dàyào** [大药, great medicine] is called **chōulián** [抽铅, extracting lead],
Firmly settling the breath to gather true lead.
The **Dàyào** [大药, great medicine] is the **Jīndān** [金丹, golden elixir]
Of **Yáng** essence transforming into **qi**."*

Before the **qi** transforms, what is produced comes from the **Dāntián** [丹田, elixir field],
Yet it is mere **qi** without form—
A subtle attachment to the outer body grants it shape,
And thus the name *Great Medicine* [大药] arises later,
So the earlier stage is called *Little Medicine* [小药], for its **qi** is small.

Once the *Golden Elixir* [金丹] is refined,
After the **qi** has transformed,
What is produced from the **Dāntián** is called *Great Medicine*.
There is indeed the tangible **qi** of true fire-pearl,
Which also emerges from the void into existence.

The Yellow Emperor spoke of:
*"Crimson Water and Mysterious Pearl"* [赤水玄珠],
Or the *Water of True-One* [真一之水],
The *Essence of True-One* [真一之精],
The *Qi of True-One* [真一之炁],
The *Lotus in the Jade Pool* [华池莲花],
The *Earth-Surging Golden Lotus* [地涌金莲],
The *Heavenly Maiden Offering Flowers* [天女献花],
The *Dragon Maiden Offering Pearls* [龙女献珠],
The *Earth-Surging Treasure Pagoda* [地涌宝塔],
The *Knife and Round Tablet* [刀圭],
The *Yellow Sprout* [黄芽],
The *True Lead* [真铅]—
These varied names all refer to the **qi** born within the **Dāntián**.
Once it forms its own tangible shape,
It does not cling to external form,
But arises solely within—
This is known and visible to the **Shénjué** [神觉, divine perception].

Upon crossing the *Two Bridges* [二桥] and passing the *Three Passes* [三关],
All becomes known and visible,
This is the fruit of liberation from birth-and-death,
And from here one attains true verification.

The *Tiānxiān Zhènglǐ* [天仙正理] says:
*"When my teacher first refined the elixir,*
*He also knew how to halt the fire,*
*Yet though he gathered the *Great Medicine* [大药] at the *Piercing Pass* [冲关],*
*He could not pass it.*
*Now I attempt it again—*
*Having traversed the path before,*
*Why should I face such perilous collapse?*

My teacher replied:
*'When the Old Master of Li [李真人] transmitted to me,*
*He revealed the utmost secret and essential aspect of the *Medicine-Fire* [药火],*
*And you could refine it upon practice.*
*Yet before the pass,*
*There is the method of the *Five Dragons Upholding the Sage* [五龙捧圣],*
*A most secret celestial principle,*
*Which only a *Heavenly Immortal* [天仙] can transmit,*
*And only a *Heavenly Immortal* [天仙] can comprehend—*
*It is not something the world can possess,*
*Nor can ordinary mortals hear of it.*
*Wait until your hundred days’ work is complete,*
*When you halt the fire and gather the *Great Medicine* [大药],*
*Then I will reveal it to you.'*

After my teacher returned to his home,
And I remained in my chamber,
I resolutely strove with fervent spirit,
Determined to succeed—
Even if I failed to become an immortal,
Even if I could not ascend to heaven!
After fifty days of practice,
The elixir was refined, the fire halted,
And I gathered the *Great Medicine*—
Yet I could not pierce the pass.

I again sought my teacher,
And he said:
*'Truly a bold and resolute seed of immortality and buddha!*
*Now come and listen to the method of *Upholding the Sage* [捧圣].*
*I have already heard it,*
*And will practice it myself—*
*In no time, the scene of halting the fire will appear,*
*And I regret not attaining it sooner.*
*Come now!*

*The *Great Medicine* does not come,*
*For the fire is not yet sufficiently strong—*
*As the Master Qiu [邱祖] said,*
*The golden essence does not yet fly.*
*I gathered and refined again,*
*And the scene of halting the fire appeared once more.*

I doubted and said:
*'It appeared before,*
*Yet when halting the fire and gathering it,*
*I did not obtain the *Great Medicine*—*
*I will wait until it appears many times,*
*Then the fire and medicine must surely be attained.'*

By the fourth appearance,
I encountered the perilous collapse,
And again strove with determination.
Then I recalled:
*'When I first refined the essence,*
*I used the scene without knowing it,*
*And was merely startled by its suddenness.'*
I quieted myself again,
And the scene appeared once more.
I awoke with a start and said:
*'The teacher spoke of halting the fire—*
*Alas, I missed it right before my eyes!*

*Again I quieted myself,*
*And the scene appeared once more,*
*Then I knew:*
*To halt the fire and gather the medicine,*
*I must seize it at the third appearance—*
*And later, not miss it in refining.*

*If I halt it at the first appearance,*
*I lose it quickly.*
*If I wait until the fourth appearance,*
*I lose it slowly.*
*To halt it neither too soon nor too late,*
*To gather the medicine and pierce the pass,*
*To transmute the **Yáng** spirit [阳神] at the critical point—*
*This is the foremost great matter at the *Ordinary-Sage Pass* [凡圣关头],*
*A trial of utmost toil and suffering.*

*With reverence and tears,*
*I recount it in detail,*
*And later exhort the Sage of Truth to caution."*

The **Xù Zhēn Jūn** in *"Drunken Thoughts of the Immortal"* says:
*"Within, the true **qi** is exchanged,*
*And breath is preserved—*
*Then **naturally**, the **Tao**’s transformation*
*Restores the youthful visage."*

An ancient song declares:
*"From **Kǎn**’s depths it arises,*
*Within the **Liè** cauldron it takes form."*

The **Xuán Yáng Zǐ** states:
*"If **Yáng** essence [日精] is joined with **Yīn** luminosity [月华],
*Then **true yán** (真铅) will surely appear in the world."*

**Mǎ Dānyáng** says:
*"When fire ignites in water, cease the **mind**’s stirrings,*
*When flowers bloom in snow, quench the **intent**’s spring."*

**Lǚ Zǔ** declares:
*"At the **origin** of life’s **qi** [受气初],*
*Exhaust its **Yáng** force—*
*Do not blame the **Tao**’s mechanisms*
*For being fully revealed."*

**Bái Yù Chán** says:
*"I grasp the **Yáng** essence of life’s **parents** [生身父母],
*To make them reunite once more."*

The *"Chapter on Revering the **Tao**"* (《崇正篇》) states:
*"Two **Yīn-Yáng** spirits [灵物] naturally converge,*
*Then **true yán** (真铅) will surely appear in the world."*

From *Zhuāngzi*:
*"Fire exists within water—*
*It will burn the **Great Block** (大块)."*

**Lù Zǐyě** says:
*"When the **Yáng** force is at its **waning** (晦尽) and the **Yīn** begins (朔来),
*The moment the medicine forms,*
*It is no longer an **ordinary** time."*

The **Shàng Yáng Zǐ** says:
*"The **first** **Yáng** force is a **rare** treasure—
*If one seeks it without losing its time,*
*One will surely attain the **rank** of **Celestial Immortal** (天仙).
*When the **age** reaches the **tidal phase** (潮候),
*It is the **Tao**’s transformation of **heaven** and **earth**.
*The **yán** (铅) meeting **Jǐ** (癸) is born,*
*It is the **Tao**’s transformation of the **human body**.
*When **heaven** and **earth**’s **Yáng** force revives,*
*All **things** arise.
*When the **human body**’s **Yáng** force is born,*
*The **true yán** (真铅) manifests.
*If one does not seize it at this moment,*
*It will later become **muddled** (混浊),*
*And the medicine will lose its **purity**.
*
*At the moment of **entering** the **inner chambers** (人室之际),
*When the **Great Work** (大用) is **at hand**,
*And the **six senses** (六根) are **calm** (泰定),
*Then one may **gather** and **refine** it.
*
*The *Yì* says:*
*'**Containing** the **auspicious**—*
*One may **stand firm** (可贞),*
*And **manifest** it **in due time** (以时发).'*
*The **Sage**’s intent*
*Lies in this **mystery**."*

**Bái Yù Chán** in *"Annotations on the **Pointing** of the **Mystic**"* (《指玄篇注》) says:
*"The **pre-heavenal** **qi** is **yán** (铅)—*
*Formless yet able to **control** **mercury** (汞).
*When **Liè** is **void** and **Kǎn** is **substantial**,
*And one **gathers** to **supplement** it,*
*The **mercury**’s essence will not **scatter** (飞走),
*Thus the **embryonic spirit** (胎神) may **congeal** and **transmute**.
*
*The **mystery** lies in the **heart** being like the **Great Void** (太虚),
*And **forgetting** both **form** and **sensory realm** (色境).
*When there is **nothing left** to forget,*
*Then one may **seek** it.
*If one desires **to stray** (横流),
*One will **never** succeed."*

**Shàng Yáng Zǐ** said:
*"To know when others’ **embryonic spirits** are **alive**,
What could be finer than the **ultimate essence** of the world?
At the **beginning of all things’ transformation and birth**,
Their reception of **yin-yang qi** lasts but a **fleeting instant**.
The **Dao of cultivation**—
To **refine pre-heavenal qi** is swiftest of all.

‘**Water clear, moon bright**—
Then the **elixir’s spirit** is newly born.’

**‘The Dao gives rise to the One Qi,**
The One Qi gives rise to **form**,
Within **form** yet holds the **original breath**—
This is the **pre-heavenal True One Qi**.’
If this **qi flows in harmony**, one becomes **human**;
If it **flows counter**, one becomes **immortal**.’*

**Lù Zǐyě** said:
*"The **Mysterious Pearl** is the **elixir’s symbol**.
The **elixir** cannot **self-generate**—
It must **respond to yang qi** to **transform and arise**.
‘**Plucked from another’s domain** and **planted in one’s own garden**,
Nurtured until **ripe**—
This is **Nature’s marvel**, not **human force**.’"*

**Qiū Chángchūn** said:
*"The **elixir** is originally **among mortal things**."*

**Shàng Yáng Zǐ** said:
*"To **age without action**—how could one **obtain the elixir**?
To **enter the chamber and extract lead**—this is **called ‘doing’**.
The **Great Concealment** in the **marketplace**—
Who could **perceive** it?
To **complete the cosmic vessel**,
One must first **establish the foundation**.
Only when one **secures the millet-sized pearl**
Is it **truly correct**.
Nine years of **sitting in forgetfulness**,
**Effortless attainment** is **broadly achieved**.
When the **path is fulfilled** to **three thousand**,
One **joys with all beings**.

If one **only claims ‘non-action’**
Without first **taking action**,
This is the **fool’s stubborn fixation**.
**Urgent words** are given
To **warn later learners**."*

**Lǔ Zǐyě** said:
*"The thief makes one unaware and unperceiving,
Yet steals what one possesses.
The method of cultivation—
It steals the **cosmic mechanisms** of Heaven and Earth,
Plunders the **vital qi** of the **killing cauldron**’s birth.

At **twenty-four**, the male’s **essence** flows freely;
At **twenty-eight**, the female’s **heavenly jade** descends.
Ah—
When meeting a **chivalrous warrior**, one must draw the sword;
Only when encountering a **kindred spirit** may the zither be plucked.
The **divine permanence** is the **first scripture** to be read."*

**Shàng Yáng Zǐ** said:
*"The thief steals the **original true-yang qi** of Heaven and Earth.
‘**Prematurely withering** the breath,
It arises from the **forging cauldron’s depths**.’
The **pre-heavenal breath** comes from **emptiness**—
To obtain this breath,
One must **bend one’s will and thoughts** in pursuit of it."*

*The **Jīn Sì Bǎo Lù** states:*
*"Forget to seek, seek to forget,
In forgetting, one sees;
In seeing, one forgets—
Then **yang** is born.
Forget to ascend, ascend to see,
In seeing, one transforms—
Then **lead** is complete.
When **lead** merges with **mercury** within,
And **essence** gathers with **spirit** without—
The **union** is achieved."*

*The **Bái Yù Chán**’s *Zhǐ Xuān Piān Zhù* says:*
*"The **one-yang qi** of Earth ascends to Heaven,
While the **one-yin qi** of Heaven descends to Earth.
When these two **qi** intermingle,
All things are born."*

**Qiú Chángchūn Zǔ** said:
*"When Heaven and Earth’s **one-yang** revives,
The human body observes the **scriptures for three days**.
When the moon is bright and pure, **lead** is born—
Afterward, no **divine connection** remains."*

*The **Língbǎo Huà Fǎ** states:*
*"The **pre-heavenal true-one qi** is called **void qi**.
The **golden embryo** is hidden in the **Kūn palace**,
Giving birth to the **golden mother** as the **elixir’s foundation**—
This is **nature**, this is the **original face**.
Before the **qi of the parents** unite,
It is **muddled and chaotic**—
Called **early confusion**, termed **yin-gold**.
After the parents **conceive their essence**,
It **flames and attaches**—
Called **original spirit**, termed **yang-lead**,
The **mother of the five metals**,
The **primordial chaos of Heaven and Earth**—
Also formed from this **thread of qi**."*

*The **Língbǎo Bì Fǎ** states:*
*"Entering the chamber to **refine**,
Chasing the **two qi** along the **Yellow Way**,
Uniting the **three surnames** in the **Primordial Palace**,
Turning the **seventy-two critical junctures**,
Gathering the **three thousand six hundred years’ true qi**,
Condensing into **elixir-black**,
Converging toward the **golden embryo**."*

*The **Língbǎo Bì Fǎ** states:*
*"One inhalation, one exhalation—**one breath**.
The inhalation is **yang**, the exhalation is **yin**.
The **seven orifices’** inhalations span **seven days**,
The **seven orifices’** exhalations span **seven nights**.
When the **golden mother’s** work is complete,
The **heavenly mechanism** stirs not,
The **spirit condenses**, the **eyes still**,
The **pulse halts**, the **heart suspends**."*

*The **Língbǎo Bì Fǎ** states:*
*"When **gathering the elixir**,
The **Dragon and Tiger** battle,
**Gold and Wood** are divided—
I gain, they lose;
I lose, they gain—
This is called **one-sided depletion**.
Only the **most saintly and divine**,
When **refining themselves to perfection**,
May achieve **breathless attainment**."*

*The **Chuán Dào Jí** states:*
*"The elixir is **gathered** from the **Nine Palaces** above,
Then **descends** into the **Yellow Court**;
**Lead** is **extracted** from the **curved river** below,
Then **lifted** to the **inner precincts**."*

*The **Chuán Dào Jí** states:*
*"When **qi** is born, **liquid** descends.
When **liquid** ascends, **qi** also ascends.
**Qi**’s birth is like the **sun’s** rising from the sea—
No mist or dew can **obscure its light**.
**Liquid**’s birth is like the **severe winter’s** killing—
No **shouting or scolding** can **withstand its chill**.
When **qi** ascends, it is like **emerald curtains**,
When **liquid** descends, it is like **sparse silk screens**."*

*The **Chuán Dào Jí** states:*
*"The **black lead**, which embraces the **Heaven-One essence** and ranks first among the five metals, is the origin.
Lead generates silver—lead is silver’s mother.
Sensing the **qi** of the **Great Sun**, and becoming the foremost among all stones, is **cinnabar**.
Cinnabar generates **mercury**—mercury is cinnabar’s child.
The most difficult to obtain is the **True Tiger** (kidney-qi), easily dissipated.
The most easily lost is the **True Dragon** (heart-liquid), for its accumulation is hard to achieve."*

*The **Chuán Dào Jí** states:*
*"If one **gathers the elixir** without applying **fire**, the elixir will dissipate and cannot be sustained.
If one applies **fire** without gathering the elixir, the **yang within yin** cannot be sustained.
The practice stops at **raising kidney-qi** and strengthening the warmth of the **lower dan** alone.
But when gathering the elixir, if one applies **fire with precise measure**, and within the process acts upon itself—borrowing **qi** to advance the **fire**—the great elixir will naturally become firm and enduring, eternally securing the **lower field**. This is called the **method of gathering and supplementing**.
**Refining mercury** to supplement the **elixir foundation** extends life and benefits longevity, making one an **Earth Immortal**.
If one further knows the **seven-and-a-half-day celestial timing** to gather the great elixir, using **original lead** to extract it, the **golden essence** will rise from the **lower field** to the **upper field** at the elbow’s side.
In general, gathering the elixir is to **add mercury**; adding mercury requires extracting **lead**—also called **moving the River Vehicle** and **walking the Dragon and Tiger**.
Once the **lead** is extracted later, the **mercury** descends from the **middle field** back to the **lower field**."*

*The **Zhōng Lǚ Chuán Dào Jí** states:*
*"At first, the **Dragon and Tiger** copulate and transform into **yellow sprouts**—this is the **Five Phases in reverse**.
Next, by extracting **lead** and adding **mercury**, one nurtures the **embryonic immortal**—this is the **Three Fields in repetition**.
If the **Five Phases** are not reversed, the **Dragon and Tiger** will not copulate.
If the **Three Fields** are not repeated, the **embryonic immortal** will lack **qi**.
Extracting **lead** and adding **mercury**—at **one hundred days**, the elixir’s power is complete;
at **two hundred days**, the **sacred embryo** is firm;
at **three hundred days**, the **embryonic immortal** is complete."*

*The **Zhōng Lǚ Chuán Dào Jí** states:*
*"The **Thousand Springs of Jade Spring**—when moved, it takes only half a day’s effort.
The **One Jar of Golden Liquid**—when transferred, it takes only a moment’s trace."*

*The **Zhōng Lǚ Chuán Dào Jí** states:*
*"Each inhalation and exhalation—**true qi** of **Heaven, Earth, and Man** circulates before the **Twelve Pavilions**.
One round trip is called **one breath**; within day and night, a person has **thirteen thousand five hundred breaths**.
If the **root is firm** and **original qi** is unharmed, within each breath one may align with the **true qi of Heaven and Earth**."*

*Zhōng Lí Zǔ says:*
*"A single point of the **original true seed**—
Entering the **dan-field**, it blooms eternal spring."*

*Zhū Yuànyù says:*
*"When the time has not yet arrived, one must **empty oneself** and await it.
When the time is near, one must **stir** and respond to it.
At the **waxing and waning phases**, **yang** is about to emerge but has not yet separated from **yin**—
the mechanism has already moved but has not yet left **stillness**.
From the **stillness of stability**, one must observe with **tenfold vigilance**.
When the **pivotal moment** is triggered, the **Great Ones** respond in harmony—
then one must **seize the gathering** with urgency.
Like the **imperial edict’s great proclamation**, issued at the proper time,
or the **laws of creation**, deployed at the right moment—
not a single instant must be delayed."*

*Zhū Yuànyù says:*
*"This **movement and stillness**—it penetrates **Heaven and Earth**, encompassing **River and Luo**.
The **River Diagram’s** numbers, fifty-five in total, cycle endlessly,
round as the **Heaven’s movement**.
The **Luo Book’s** positions—four cardinals and four pairs—
are governed by the central five, square as the **Earth’s stillness**.
Man is the **heart of the great earth**—
the space between **Heaven and Earth** is the **human heart**,
as **Shào Zǐ** said: the **most profound subtlety** between **movement and stillness**—
the **ultimate mystery of Heaven, Earth, and Man**."*

*Zhū Yuànyù says:*
*"When the **season arrives**, the **great elixir** is born."*

Then, in haste, take it—with **true intent** as the mediator—
as the **Phoenix returns**, blending with the **Dark Mother**,
slowly ascending from the **Kun furnace** into the **dry cauldron**.
There are countless operations: **absorbing, licking, gathering, resting**.

Zhū Yuànyù says:
*"At the **Dark Mother’s** first union, the **great elixir** is about to be born—
right at the juncture of **Hài-Zǐ** (11–1 o’clock),
where **movement and stillness** meet—
the **most subtle mechanism of Heaven and Earth**.
Even the sages cannot fathom it."*

Zhū Yuànyù says:
*"The **preheavenal qi** originally arises from **emptiness-nothingness**.
One must **sincerely commit**—**empty** and await it—
until the **six senses are utterly still**, not a thought arising,
then it may resonate.
Yet this **‘thoughtlessness’** is not the dullness of wood and stone,
but **ever-present stillness**, never straying from the **norm**.
This **thought of thoughtlessness**—this is **right awareness**.
When **right awareness** is ever-present,
only then can one **attain the preheavenal qi**,
and have the moment of **obtaining the elixir**."*

Zhū Yuànyù says:
*"When gathering the elixir, **true intent** must **urgently press**—
as the two **essences unite**, right at the **precarious void**,
one must then **seal the earthly gate**,
**gathering the true qi**—not a whisper may escape."*

Lǚ Zǔ’s *Golden Jade Scripture* says:
*"Seize the moment before **yin-yang** compare,
and **steal back the return-to-origin qi**—
exhausting this **profoundest technique**,
shedding the dust of illusion to pierce the **mystic pass**—
this is the **ultimate essence of the male Kan, female Li**,
emerging from the **most primordial palace**,
obtained at the **child hour** as the **crimson water pearl**,
**emerald nectar dew**."*

*The Golden Jade Scripture* says:
*"Act with **my** being,
employ **its** Dao."*

The **crimson water pearl** nourishes the **Kan** of the **water of the tenth stem (癸)**, residing beneath the **flame** that binds the **emerald lotus canopy (青莲)**.

When **Dao/Way** is **held in guard (守)**, one must respond with **fusing warmth (融融)** and **serene purity (清净)**.
When **Dao/Way** is **released (離)**, one must respond with **distant breadth (遥遥)** and **breathing harmony (呼吸)**.

*The Golden Jade Scripture* says:
*"**Dao/Way** within me is **forgotten in the body (忘體)**,
**Dao/Way** beyond me is **effortless wandering (逍遙)**."*

*The Golden Jade Scripture* says:
*"**Steal** the **Great Ultimate (太極)** in a single moment—
hundreds, thousands, tens of millions, billions.
**Steal** the **Great Ultimate (太極)** in a billion *kalpas*—
**observe** it from above and below."*

*The Jade Scripture* says:
*"The **source (源)** in the **Heavenly realm (上)**,
**pours** the **sacred vein (聖脈)** into **clarity (清)**.
The **source (源)** in the **Earthly realm (下)**,
**rises** the **numinous spring (靈泉)** from the **Kan (坎)**.
The **source (源)** in **humans (人)**,
**circulates** the **blood and qi (血氣)** within the **body (身)**.
The **source (源)** in **things (物)**,
**aligns** the **wandering transformations (逍遙)** with **time (時)**.
The **source (源)** in **Dao/Way (道)**,
**distinguishes** the **teachings of transformation (教化)** between **evil and righteousness (邪正)**.
The **source (源)** in **nature (性)**,
**turns** the **river chariot (河車)** in **harmony with yielding and welcoming (順迎)**.
The **source (源)** in **time (時)**,
**fixes** the **tides of the child and horse hours (潮汐)** at **子 (zi)** and **午 (wu)**.
The **source (源)** within **me (我)**,
**controls** the **luminous jade (澄碧)** through **yin-yang (陰陽)**."*

*The Golden Jade Scripture* says:
*"When **qi** **unites with its source (合源)**,
how does the **source (源)** **differentiate (別)**?
The **source (源)** is **clear (清)** and **Dao/Way** **arises (生)**,
the **source (源)** is **murky (渾)** and **Dao/Way** **fades (息)**."*

*The Golden Jade Scripture* says:
*"**Dark and vast (穹穹)**—
**body (體)** is formed from **void union (虚合)**,
and when the **body (體)** is complete, the **void (虚)** returns.
When **Dao/Way** is complete, there is **no end (無已)**."*

*The True Dao Chanting Scripture* says:
*"When **my** mind **not a single thought arises (一念不起)**,
then **void whiteness (虚白)** **naturally generates (自然相生)**.
At this time, **semen (精)** is **true essence (真精)**,
**qi** is **true qi (真氣)**,
**spirit (神)** is **true spirit (真神)**.
**Use** the **true essence (真精)**, **true qi (真氣)**, **true spirit (真神)** in **undivided unity (浑合为一)**.
**Merge spirit with qi (神合氣)**, **stillness and nourishment (靜養)** as the **practice (功)**.
**Merge qi with spirit (氣合神)**, **holding and guiding (操持)** as the **key (要)**.
**Merge essence with spirit (精合神)**, **clarity and voidness (清虚)** as the **foundation (本)**."*

*The True Dao Chanting Scripture* says:
*"When **stillness and cultivation (靜修)** are **wondrous (既妙)**,
they **naturally generate** **link by link (节节相生)**,
**head by head (头头是道)**.
**Boundless wondrous realms (无穷妙境)** flow from **primordial intent (先天一意)**,
not merely **empty knowledge (空空之知)** or **void awareness (虚虚之觉)**—
there is indeed **true elixir (真药)** and **true benefit (真受用)**.
**Everlasting vision (一元长见)** and **revival of all phenomena (万象回春)**,
**cannot be described with words or depicted with forms (不可以言语形容也)**."*

*The True Dao Chanting Scripture* says:
*"**Elemental essence (元精)** **dissolves (溶溶)**,
**elemental spirit (元神)** **leaps (跃跃)**,
**elemental qi (元气)** **soars (腾腾)**—
the **three primal elements (三元)** are **complete (具矣)**."*

*The True Dao Chanting Scripture* says:
*"**Postnatal intent (后天之意)** is called **intent (意)**,
**primordial intent (先天之意)** is called **spirit (神)**.
Where **spirit (神)** resides, **qi (氣)** follows.
**Qi (氣)** **depends on spirit (神)** to **generate (生)**,
and also **depends on spirit (神)** to **subside (息)**."*

*The True Dao Chanting Scripture* says:
*"Having **known** this **Dao/Way (道)**,
**strive diligently** in **secret cultivation (勤修密印)**.
**Mingled and indistinct (混混沌沌)**,
**vast and mysterious (鸿鸿蒙蒙)**.
What is **spirit (神)**, what is **qi (氣)**, what is **essence (精)**?
If **spirit (神)**, then **qi (氣)** and **essence (精)** are **present (在焉)**.
If **qi (氣)**, then **spirit (神)** and **essence (精)** are **present (在焉)**.
If **essence (精)**, then **spirit (神)** and **qi (氣)** are **present (在焉)**.
Like **sugar** or **honey (如糖如蜜)**,
like **powder entering grain (似粉入麦)**,
before the **five phases (五行)** **manifest (未兆)**,
when the **three talents (三才)** **remain undivided (未判)**,
this is the **elixir ancestor (丹祖)**,
the **Great Ultimate (太極)** itself.
**Intent (意)** **before intent (先)** is **no intent (无意)**,
**intent (意)** **after intent (后)** is **no intent (无意)**—
only the **middle (中间)** is **obtained (得)**,
a **single, solitary true intent (单单—个真意)**.
**Adopting yang and forming the embryo (采阳结胎)**,
**shedding the body and exiting the spirit (脱体出神)**,
both **rely on it (俱藉之)**.
At the **moment of union (交会之际)**,
the **entire body (遍体)** **fuses harmoniously (融和)**,
like **warm springtime qi (暖春天气)**,
or **the drowsy awakening in deep sleep (熟睡方醒)**,
with the **chest realm (胸境)** **brightly open (洞然)**.
What is this **fruit of union (交会果)**?
It is **spirit (神)**, it is **essence (精)**, it is **qi (氣)**—
yet **not essence (非精)**, **not qi (非氣)**, **not spirit (非神)**—
**named as Dao (名之为道)**, **seen as elixir (見之为丹)**.
It is **likened to the Great Ultimate (拟议之为太极)**.
**One inhalation, one exhalation (一呼一吸)**,
**penetrates** the **mechanism of qi (氣機)**.
**One movement, one stillness (一动一静)**,
**harmonizes** with **creation (造化)**.
**Revolving yin-yang (回陰陽)** within **one pitcher (一壶之内)**,
**encompassing** the **sun and moon (羅日月)** within **half a grain of millet (半黍之中)**.
The **Great Dao (大道)** is **profoundly mysterious (冥冥)**,
the **Great Ultimate (太极)** **flows** as **refined essence (流精)**.
The **heart contains** the **primordial transformations (包元化)**,
**qi** **circulates** the **great pivot (运鸿钧)**.
Ascending to the **Heavenly Court (上朝苍昊)**,
descending to **cleanse the dark depths (下扫幽阴)**.
**Revolving winds and blending (回風混合)**,
**hundred days’ practice (百日功)** is **efficacious (靈)**.
**Heavenly immortals (天仙)** and **earthly immortals (地仙)**,
**Water Kings (水王)** and **Mountain Lords (山君)**,
**all ascend** the **Great Aspiration (同登大愿)**,
**broadly liberating** all **sentient beings (廣度眾生)**.
**Winds and clouds, dragons and tigers (風雲龍虎)**,
**magpies and phoenixes, penguins and unicorns (叭喳鵬麟)**,
**constantly attend** at **my** side,
**aiding** the **turning of the Dharma Wheel (助转法轮)**.
When **lustful thoughts** **arise (淫心才举)**,
**true qi (真氣)** **scatters (分崩)**."*

*The True Dao Chanting Scripture* says:
*"The **qi** that **immortals gather (仙家所采之氣)**,
is the **one point of numinous light (一点靈光)** since **Primordial Origin (元始)**—
**undivided and fused (浑融周遍)**,
the **Great Harmony (太和)** of **absolute truth (至真)**,
yet **indeed without substance (实无有物)**."*

Zhang Sanfeng’s *Essentials of Golden Elixir* says:
*"The **earlier stages** are **complete (前功已周)**,
the **elixir furnace (丹鼎)** is **within the chamber (在室)**.
**Focus** on **waiting for three days (专侯三日)**,
when the **moon emerges** in the **regal direction (庚方)**—
this is when the **herbal vitality (药苗)** **first arises (初生)**,
and **one must diligently observe (正好用心审察)**.
**Entrust** the **Yellow Mother (黄婆)** to **convey (传送)** it,
so that the **Golden Father (金公)** **does not lose the moment (失刻)**,
and the **crowds (姹众)** **do not exceed the deadline (过期)**.
**Guard against** the slightest **deviation (差毫厘)**,
**do not err** in the **great matter (大事)**.
Thus the **sage** **transfers** the **movement of a year’s qi (一年之氣運)**,
**urging** it into **a single moment (促在一时)**.
Again, **dividing** that **moment (一时)** into **six watch periods (六候)**,
the **first two periods (前二候)** **yield the elixir (得药)**,
the **last four periods (后四候)** have **another marvelous use (另有妙用)**.
**Cultivators of the elixir (修丹之士)**,
can they **not be cautious (可不慎与)**?

Already **knowing** the **other schools’ method of vitalizing the child hour (活子时)**,
**urgently distinguish** the **clear or murky source of the water (辨伊水源清浊)**.
When **golden light first appears (金光初现)**,
and the **moon shines in the midnight hour (月色中宵)**,
**sit still** at the **four cardinal directions (坐定四正)**,
**face toward** the **direction of birth (朝生位)**.
Even if **dragons swallow the sword of the crane (龙含鹤剑)**,
**more importantly, prevent the tiger’s movement (虎动)** and **spirit’s agitation (神修)**.
**Distinguish guest and host (分宾主)** and **enter the nuptial chamber (而入洞房)**,
**pairing Heaven and Earth (配天地)** while **forming the Tai (泰) hexagram (卦)**.
**Heart to heart, solemnly cautious (心心笃慎)**,
**observing** the **pulse of intent (察意脉)** for **speed or slowness (疾迟)**.
**Mouth to mouth, transmitted (口口相传)**,
**determining** the **floating and sinking (定浮沉)** for **urgency or leisure (缓急)**.
**Concentrate spirit (凝神)** and **stabilize breath (定息)**,
**forgetting self and others (人我两忘)**.
**Light as a key and fan (橐钥轻扇)**,
**gentle as the gentle wind (巽风慢鼓)**.
**Ignite** the **fire talisman of lead and mercury (发起铅汞火符)**,
**adjust and harmonize** the **civil and martial (文武)** to **align with Heaven (同天)**.
**Gradually prompt (款款催之)** and **earnestly await (切切候之)**.
**Seek first** the **silver and jade pool within the water (水中银玉池先觅)**,
**retain** the **mercury and gold furnace within the vermilion (朱里汞金鼎方留)**.
Only in **this fleeting instant (只在须臾)**,
**cannot be divided** even by **a moment (难分顷刻)**.
**Above and below respond (上下相应)**,
**inner and outer correspond (内外资符)**.
**One’s own awareness (自觉)** of the **numinous root (灵根)** **fires (火发)**,
**collect** the **pearl from the ocean’s depths (收拾海底珠)** and **return (还)**—
**quickly act (速宜下手)**,
**do not hesitate (切莫留情)**."*

Swiftly, the **true essence** from the left kidney is **circulated** to form a single drop,
then at the **Wu Gate** it meets the **half-expanded golden water**,
forging a **single elixir pellet**—
**nine transformations** complete its success.

When the **two substances** meet, they must **align perfectly**,
when the **three families** converge, **harmony** is **naturally** achieved.

In **mere moments**, the **true lead** remains in the furnace,
while the **fierce fire tempers** its **sharpness**.

Hasten to **stir and refine**,
**boldly** add and **draw forth**—
the **Numinous Father** may now **turn over**,
the **Holy Mother** **teaches separation** from the body.
Swiftly board the **Heavenly Barge**,
and **cross the Magpie Bridge** nine times nine.

Lightly **raise** the **posterior gold essence** ninety times,
**circulate** it to the **Milky Way**,
then **add nine more cycles**,
returning it to the **mud-ball**.

If **too slow**, in **fleeting moments** it descends to the **elixir field**.

At that time, **garlic** may be **planted in the nostrils**,
**tears** may be **drawn into the throat**—
when the **Jade Chamber** receives the elixir,
the **Yellow Lady** guides it down from the **upper palace**.

Once the **golden liquid returns**,
the **Cowherd** is summoned to **return it to the earthen tripod**.

Now, **calm as still waters**,
from this day forth, **the land prospers**, **the people thrive**,
**qi condenses**, **spirit solidifies**,
**soul and shadow** are **steadied**—
the body **harmonized**, **spring light** fills the eyes,
the **Heavenly Sovereign** at **ease**, all **spirits** obey.

Having **obtained the union of lead and mercury**,
one must **firmly establish** the **heart-mind coiling**.

Having **seized Heaven’s secret**, one must **return to the Transformative**.
The **wonder of elixir-gathering** lies here.

**Drawing and refining**, **bathing**—
all methods are **detailed** below,
leaving **no residue**.

Zhang Sanfeng’s *"The Rootless Tree"* states:
*"Without yin and yang, the Dao is incomplete.
The whole is separated by wood—
mercury between lead,
yin scarce, yang solitary, each on its own side.
Mortals pair yin and yang as male and female,
begetting sons and grandsons, generation after generation.
To follow is mundane; to invert, divine—
only the reversal in between."*

*"The Rootless Tree"* continues:
*"The eastern maiden, the western youth,
as husband and wife enter the nuptial chamber.
The Yellow Lady urges them to drink the kshira-pak (clarified butter) wine—
one day, lifting the veil, a voice of intoxication.
This elixir recipe, the soul-reviving elixir,
the life-restoring medicine of the Medicine King.

Born in the *Kun* (earth) position, it is human.
Plucking the flower’s stem, harvesting its heart—
layer upon layer, blooming with spring’s splendor.

When stripped and reborn, it has a fixed term.
Lead blooms appear, at the end of *geng* (癸),
once more, the western garden brims with blossoms.
Under the moon’s fading light, gathering the remnants,
then mending the robe in the morning sun’s glow.
This mechanism—few in the world know it;
one must carefully ponder it with the immortals.

Gazing at the moon, lost in its radiance,
golden essence flourishes, dazzling the eyes like flowers.
With hands reaching for the clouds, ascending the moon’s ladder,
plucking the first branch of primordial heaven.

The lead crucible warms, revealing its luminous treasure—
on the golden bridge, gazing toward the *Qujiang*,
in the moon’s glow, the sun is clearly seen.
At the furnace’s edge, the scene unfolds before you."*

*The Golden Locker’s Precious Record* states:
*"Great light penetrates—
employing the mechanism of entry and exit."*

Master Shao’s *"Poems from the Peaceful Nest"*:
*"The Sage’s deeds are without difficulty to inherit,
a priceless pearl lies only in the depths."*

Master Shao’s *"Poems from the Peaceful Nest"*:
*"The wine drawn from the flower’s shadow glows red and smooth—
how could one bear not to drink and return drunk before it?"*

Master Shao’s *"Poems from the Peaceful Nest"*:
*"Such meaning is difficult to name,
for fear that mortals all remain unaware."*

*The Chant of the Dao’s Truth* says:
*"The two characters ‘yang spirit’—
do not regard them solely as pertaining to the human body.
Born from Heaven, it is this yang spirit.
Born from Earth, it is this yang spirit.
Born from sun, moon, stars, and constellations,
from embryonic, oviparous, wet, and dry transformations,
from flying, burrowing, moving, and vegetating beings—
all are this yang spirit.
This yang spirit is the *Taiji*."*

*The Chant of the Dao’s Truth* says:
*"Zhang Wuzhang’s intent serves as the mediator’s words,
though sparse, they remain unclear.
His original intent stems from the heart,
manifesting in nature—
thus, there is true heart, and only then true nature.
With true nature, only then is there true intent,
which is called the *primordial single intent*.
Before the primordial forms took shape,
no traces were revealed—
how could there be such a thing as intent?
When seated in stillness,
the mind empties, vast and luminous,
without sediment, without knowledge—
this is the primordial nature.
From this, a single point of true intent descends from the void,
like the *Taiji* circle, where yin and yang are conceived;
like the *Fuxi* single stroke, where the two transformations arise—
thus, it is called the *primordial single intent*.
When paired with water and fire,
when guiding lead and mercury,
its use is unfailingly effective.
The elixir’s completion is all this single intent in motion."*

*The Chant of the Dao’s Truth* says:
*"A wandering intent is not intent—
it is roving thoughts and delusions.
Intent is what truly arises from the heart,
intent arising, the heart returns to emptiness—
thus, it is said: *having intent yet as if without intent*.
Its function is vast indeed!
Initially, when yang is born, it is intent.
After its birth, when harvesting primordial yang, it is intent.
After harvesting, when uniting in the divine chamber, it is intent.
After union, when sent to the Yellow Court, it is intent.
Not only this—
when the yang spirit emerges, it is intent.
After emerging, when riding the void and commanding the wind, it is intent.
Roaming the celestial realm, returning to the divine chamber—
it is intent.
The function of intent is vast indeed!"*

*The Records of the Union of Immortal and Buddha* state:
*"Reflecting inward and observing within—
this is the wondrous function of true intent.
For the original spirit remains unmoving as its essence,
true intent communicates through sensation—
both are one substance.
It may be called ‘spirit,’ or ‘intent’—
thus, true intent is the true awareness of emptiness,
the subtle understanding of mutual recognition."*

*The Records of the Union of Immortal and Buddha* state:
*"When refining essence, true intent observes the hundred days of refining spirit.
When refining qi, true intent observes the ten months of refining qi.
When refining spirit, true intent observes the three years of refining spirit.
From beginning to end, it never departs from this inner observation and reflection."*

*The Records of the Union of Immortal and Buddha* state:
*"The light of both pupils is where the true intent of the spirit resides.
Where the pupils’ light reaches, there the true intent arrives.
Qiu Zu said:
‘The Great Elixir is not difficult to seek—
daytime, gaze at the central field; nighttime, guard and preserve.
Water and fire naturally separate above and below,
a cluster of life’s intent lies within the twin pupils.’"*

*The Records of the Union of Immortal and Buddha* state:
*"Generally, when gathering elixir,
by the third or fourth day, true intent is on the verge of stabilization—
at the moment of obtaining the elixir’s scene, it appears in sequence.
By the fifth or sixth day, true breath stabilizes,
and the great elixir emerges—
thus, the seven-day cycle is but a rough estimate.
When the elixir forms, the six senses tremble,
the *dantian* burns like fire,
both kidneys simmer like boiling water,
the eyes emit golden light,
a phoenix arises behind the ears,
an eagle cries within the brain,
the body surges, the nose twitches—
these are all signs of obtaining the elixir."*

**Volume Seven: Nurturing the Returned Elixir**

「Master Shangyang said: *"Once the Daoist elixir (刀圭) has entered the mouth,
one must circulate one’s own true fire to nourish it.
At the moment when the wind (氣) stirs the fire,
suddenly one feels the true qi (夹脊真气) at the spine’s junction surging upward into the *dantian* (泥丸),
a dripping sound arising—
from the head, as if something were pressing against the upper brain (脑中),
then in a short while, like sparrows’ eggs, grain by grain descending from the palate into the *zhonglou* (重楼),
tasting like water, fragrant and sweet,
with a flavor unparalleled—
this is the verification.

When obtaining the golden liquid elixir (金液还丹),
one slowly swallows it back into the *dantian* (丹田),
and from then onward, it ceases not.

In idle self-observation,
the viscera and bowels are distinctly visible, as if illuminated by a candle,
and gradually, golden light envelops the body."*

*The Pulse Gazing* scripture states:
*"At the time when one circulates mercury (汞) to meet lead (铅),
crossing the *Queqiao* (鹊桥) to the east,
through the *Weilü* (尾闾) guiding the *Mingmen* (命门),
passing the *Jiaxiang* (夹香),
entering the *dantian* (泥丸),
pouring into the twin pupils (双目),
descending the *Jinqiao* (金桥),
crossing the *Yinhé* (银河),
and blending within the *Zhonggong* (中宫),
it is murky as mist shrouding a mountain,
rustling as wind and rain striking suddenly,
dimly as the first stirrings of a daytime dream,
and vast as rising from a bath—
this is the true sight of the spirit (精神) merging in obscurity,
the qi (气) returning, when the body’s yin (阴) essence disperses completely.
It is not mere metaphor.

Master Shao said:
*'When yin and yang begin their subtle transformation,
the heavens and earth stir and revolve in turn—
In that fleeting moment of most wondrous appearance,
How can one’s practice be spoken of?'*

This is the true body’s creation and actual realization.

*"Gathering the undifferentiated essence (炁) of the two principles (二仪),
seizing the primal vitality (精) of the Dragon and Tiger at their first union—
this refers to the moment when the two agents (二候) harmonize and the elixir forms.
At this juncture, the mechanism moves with a resonant hum (籁鸣),
yin and yang meet for the first time,
lead and mercury begin to blend,
the male and female align—
the true sight of the vital essence (滋液) moistening and nourishing,
when the yang elixir first enters the earthen cauldron (土釜),
and the mutual response occurs.

Heaven and earth in vaporous union (氤氲),
male and female in copulative essence,
the spirit (神) reaches its fourfold apex (四达),
coiling at the celestial boundaries, embracing the earth.
Like smoke, like mist, like dew, like lightning—
ineffable, the masculine vitality (雄扬) spreads and disseminates,
the feminine yin (雌阴) consolidates and transforms,
and the single breath (一气) flows unimpeded.

The essence of the five agents (二五之精),
subtly merging and congealing—
once congealed for long,
it reveals the true form.
Thus, when the practice is pure and unadulterated,
the elixir and substances do not waste away,
the fire and timing do not falter,
and the golden elixir ripens—
one attains the true Dao."*

*The Clarification of Cultivation* states:
*"Someone asked: ‘How does one recognize the moment of death and rebirth?’
The reply was: ‘At the exact hour of *Zhèngzǐ* (子时),
this is the critical moment for seizing life (接命).
When true lead is cast into mercury,
lead and mercury blend in harmony,
one must fear that both will become extinguished,
and sink into the void of chaos (混沌之窍).
A single careless breath,
and the great elixir will leak away.
This is the most vital pass—
seizing life occurs here,
and harming life also occurs here.
Initially, it is not the flames of ordinary fire,
forged with fierce cooking and refining,
that can extract the gold from its ore.
Later, it is not the divine fire (神火),
for gentle warmth and nourishment surround it,
that can alter the elixir’s nature.
‘Advancing fire to extract lead,
retiring fire to add mercury—
the method mirrors the sun and moon,
balancing water and fire,
all focused on harmony.
*The Scripture of the Seal* says:
*"Harmony brings alignment, the path smooth and unerring."*
And again:
*"Each attains its own harmony, and both reveal their signs.
Achieving central harmony (中和) sets heaven and earth in order,
and all things flourish."*
The meaning is profound indeed!"*

The elixir returns to the Yellow Court, sealed within the earthen tripod—
when the foundation is firm, the embryo will not leak.
Move the dragon’s flowing pearls with fire to match it,
and the spirit-embryo will take form.
As the *Scripture of the Seal* says:
*"Send it back to the sealed earthen tripod,
then pair it with the flowing pearls—
this is the proper alignment."*

Green Mist Master said:
*"Firm the foundation so the embryo does not leak—
transformation occurs in an instant."*

How then does one firm the foundation?
The *Scripture of the Seal* says:
*"Withdraw the *li* qi to contain the *ying* and *wei*,
and *kan* need not rely on hearing.
*Fui* unites without speech,
keeping silent to follow the Original Unity."*

Master Shangyang said:
*"When ordinary people copulate,
they jolt the bones of the body,
agitate the marrow of the limbs—
as soon as desire stirs,
the mind-sovereign trembles,
the Three Corpses rise above,
the Seven Spirits collapse below,
and only then does the essence ascend from the calves,
pass through the five viscera,
rise to the *niwan*,
and descend with the marrow,
through the *double pass* and *external kidney*,
to the place of copulation—
this is the five turbidities of the mundane path,
the natural order of the Dao.

But the Golden Elixir is otherwise—
it practices inverted methods,
holds the inverted path.
The great adept, having refined himself thoroughly,
remains unmoved in body and mind,
the soul and spirit subdued,
desire not intruding,
the essence and qi full—
like a wealthy household,
where gold and jade abound everywhere.
When the first *yáng* stirs,
the primordial true lead approaches,
and yet my body’s essence and qi remain still.
I simply take a drop of true mercury nearby in the lower kidney
to greet it—
this is the *short advance* of the fore-stage.

Once the true lead has crossed the Magpie Bridge,
mercury and lead merge,
then follow the lead as it ascends—
the three revolving wheels pass through the double pass,
the spinal column, and the *niwan*,
traversing the Nine Palaces,
entering the twin eyes,
descending the Golden Bridge,
passing the Red Tower,
entering the Vermilion Palace,
and returning to the Yellow Court’s divine chamber—
this is the *long retreat* of the later stage."*

Master Shangyang said:
*"The *niwan* says:
*'If my practice lasts one year,
the six pulses will cease, and the breath returns to the root.'*
Laozi says:
*'Devote the breath to supreme softness,
and you may be like an infant.'*
Both speak of nourishment.

Nourishment means
weakening the limbs,
dulling the senses—
all day like a fool, yet never straying,
never to be separated for an instant.
Like a hen brooding her eggs,
the warm breath must never cease,
and the work of extraction and addition will naturally appear.

Extraction and addition mean:
after the lead restrains the mercury,
gradually move the fire each day,
slowly adding mercury—
as mercury increases, lead decreases,
until the lead is exhausted,
the mercury dries,
and becomes cinnabar—
the pure *yang* essence of the Golden Elixir.

At this point, the breath transforms into seed—
this is the infant,
this is the *yang* spirit."*

The *Emerald Emptiness Chapter* says:
*"At first, the spinal pass opens,
then the bladder burns like fire.
Within, the two kidneys boil like soup—
now stir the heart’s source!
The heart and kidneys exchange water and fire,
yet who separates the metal and wood?
The Yellow Court’s breath dwells in the central palace,
governing all phenomena, the heart holds sway.
The water source is clear as a jade mirror—
who makes the River Vehicle move like a boat?
In a flash, flames blaze and extinguish—

The Dragon roars, the Tiger howls—
husband and wife in perfect harmony.
The jade cauldron simmers with elixir,
the golden furnace blazes with fire.

Thunder crashes, lightning streaks—
shaking heaven and earth.
A hundred meridians surge,
the three passes pierce through.

The dark pearl takes form,
the Supreme Unity embraces the True.
The *dantian* wind stirs,
the Vermilion Palace glows with moonlight,
the cinnabar field warms with mist,
the *guhai* sea ripples clear.

Refining the Returning Elixir—
easy as turning one’s palm.
Henceforth, the Celestial Pass is in hand,
the Earthly Axis moves with the heart,
and one may wield the *lingqi* banner by day,
record divine herbs by night.

Warming the Sacred Embryo,
forming the Red Child.

Zhuangzi said:
*"All comes down to this single effort—
eternal boundless joy preserved."*

This is the foundation of the Dao,
the root of virtue,
the lineage of Dragon and Tiger,
the origin of lead and mercury.
One fire gathered,
eight waters converging—
the gate where ten thousand spirits assemble,
the source of the Golden Elixir’s marvels,
the pivotal moment of returning to the root and reclaiming life.

Once this is known,
desire need not be abandoned—
the mind stilled of its own accord,
the spirit clarified without effort.
No thought arises,
ten thousand illusions dissolve,
the body rides the *fuxiao* winds,
the spirit wanders the boundless void.

Only then does one understand:
the Dao’s breeze and moon’s purity—
all revealing the workings of lead and mercury,
the green waters and blue mountains—
fully disclosing the essence of Dragon and Tiger.

*The Sea Guest’s Treatise* says:
*"Mercury—
the accumulated *yin* qi, the essence of the dark waters,
encountering myriad transformations to form spirit,
serving the five metals to manifest soul.
Heavier than gold, purer than dust,
it lies before one’s eyes—
what difficulty is there in seeing it?"*

Zhuangzi said:
*"Lead is like a form,
mercury like its shadow.
Mercury is the vital essence, the refined soul of lead—
each possesses its own body,
mutually harboring its root.
The Five Phases interbreed,
metal and water generate one another.
When qi is obtained and transformations unfold,
only then does the supreme medicine form."*

Again he said:
*"It is but mercury, one substance,
flowing through all the celestial phases."*

And again:
*"Mercury is the true substance—
first flesh, then bone."*

The completed medicine is but mercury,
borrowing the womb of divine water
to become the powder of purple gold.

An ancient song says:
*"Mercury is the true elixir of immortals,
transmitted from above—
suppressed fire is hard to tame.
When the River Vehicle forms purple powder,
the purple powder instantly becomes the Golden Elixir.
The true method of the Golden Elixir has no equal—
mercury alone is profound.
The *daoji* blade verifies its transformation—
taken, it grants no death,
but the boat of immortality."*

And again:
*"Reverse-extracting yields mercury,
the Returning Elixir reverts to sand.
Within the womb, five colors are received,
a full moon brings the yellow sprout.
Lost paths cannot be seen—
face-to-face, it’s the edge of the world.
If you reach the River Vehicle’s domain,
this alone is the realm of the immortals."*

The *Gui Zhong Zhinan* states:

*"Those who cultivate the Elixir wish to restore their nature, return to their origin, regenerate the five viscera, and re-establish their form—
to give birth to substance from non-substance,
and form the sacred embryo.
Its secret lies here:
Concentrate the qi until it is supremely soft,
like an infant.
Eliminate distractions and still the mind,
quietly preserving the One.

External thoughts do not intrude,
internal thoughts do not arise.
The whole day is a state of primordial chaos,
as if still in the womb.
When the spirit aligns with the qi,
and the qi harmonizes with the spirit,
the spirit condenses into qi,
and the qi abides as spirit.

In the realm of still repose,
it seems as though in a land of nothingness—
the Heavenly Heart in profound darkness,
attending to a single orifice,
like a hen brooding her egg,
or a fish in water.
Exhale to the root,
inhale to the calyx,
endlessly sustained.

Then guard the single breath within the embryo,
guarding nothing—
the true breath abides of itself,
vanishing as if nonexistent.
Yet within the heart’s boundless void,
one consciousness becomes the sovereign of transformation."*

Lu Xixing remarked:
*"After attaining the One,
the chaos reintegrates as the Supreme Ultimate—
no need to distinguish east, west, south, or north,
only vigilance at the pass.
If the mind wanders,
beware lest all prior effort be lost.
Should one indulge a fleeting surge of passion,
they forget the toil of former days—
and thus ruin the great work."*

The Master of Upper Yang said:
*"A single grain of elixir—
how difficult to obtain!
Exhausting every hardship and toil,
only then can it be acquired.
Once obtained, it is a fortunate preservation of this precious life.
Then one should reside in seclusion, nurturing and refining it with care—
reducing it again and again,
desiring the mind to fade while the will must rise,
laboring with fervor while the realm is forgotten.
Before the elixir is used,
one walks the true Daoist path.
If one has already obtained the elixir,
they hold the heart of complete emptiness—
then all affairs and things
do not concern them, and there is no peril,
until the work is complete, the fire is full, yet they remain undeterred."*

Tao Suzi said:
*"I have often embraced the true *qi* of harmony,
nurturing the settled essence of the Primordial Spirit.
The method of nurturing lies in nothing more than simplicity and detachment.
Simplicity and detachment mean
attaining emptiness and focusing the spirit,
pure and unadulterated,
following nature’s course to preserve it.

At the moment when the golden essence congeals,
all meridians return to their source,
breathing ceases,
and the daily spirit and monthly spirit
halt their wheels as if life were about to end.
Ending and then reborn,
the Master of Purple Clarity speaks of *'This death is now true life.'*
When the nurturing is complete,
the body transforms into Pure Yang—
then the elixir is formed, the medicine is ready."*

White Jade Shaan said:
*"If one can, within the settled stillness,
embrace the harmonious *qi*,
guard the true essence of the One,
then they seal the furnace and secure the crossing to proceed with the fire’s stages.
The spirit is the fire,
the *qi* is the medicine—
refining the medicine with fire to form the elixir
is the same as mastering the *qi* with the spirit to attain the Dao."*

*The Daoist-Buddhist Concordance on the Analects* says:
*"During the ten months of refining, one must hold the call.
At this time, drowsiness and distraction are easy,
scattered thoughts prevail while inner stillness is scarce—
then the method of refining *qi* to transform the spirit is used to supplement the spirit.
When the spirit is full, one does not think of sleep;
when the spirit is settled, one does not think of wandering.
Drowsiness and distraction gradually diminish,
stillness grows until the Great Stillness arrives.
Without *qi* and breath,
breath has no coming or going—
this is called *xi zhu* [息住]."*

*The Daoist-Buddhist Concordance on the Analects* says:
*"The ten months’ work requires
the spirit and *qi* to be clear and bright,
the will and mind to be bold and fierce.
Day and night, one must diligently labor within stillness,
stillness continuing without pause,
not a single breath or instant without being in breath-stillness—
then naturally one attains the Great Stillness without breath.
On the day of Great Stillness,
it is the day of the embryo’s completion.
The spirit-embryo having formed,
it finally manifests and emerges—
this is the natural order."*

*The Daoist-Buddhist Concordance on the Analects*:
Q: *"What is stillness?"*
A: *"The Master of Double Yang said:
*'Breath and stillness correspond,
pulse ceases, *qi* stops.
Stillness generates stillness—
within Great Stillness, the Primordial *qi* of the First Heaven arises from emptiness.'*
He also said:
*'Within stillness, knowing movement—
this is transformation.'*
Qiu Zu said:
*'If the breath has even a hair’s breadth of unsettledness,
it is not one’s own life to possess.'*
Xue Zixian said:
*'Stillness and breath refine True Lead.'*
Xinglin said:
*'Within stillness, the elixir is seen to form.'*
Danyang said:
*'The practice must never cease—
stillness and breath are the sacred embryo.'*
The Most High said:
*'Turning the spirit into stillness,
one attains the Supreme True.'*
*The Scripture of the Martial Granny’s Heart* says:
*'Knowing to guard the original true body,
one can further refine the Great Stillness,
until form and spirit are both perfected.'*
The Celestial Sovereign of Yuan Shi says:
*'Breath depends on stillness,
nature settled, life preserved.'*
Ziyang says:
*'Only stillness can refine the elixir—
without stillness, Yang does not arise.
After Yang arises,
without stillness, the elixir does not congeal.'*
*The Collection of Central Harmony* says:
*'Nine years and three months of constant stillness—
this is the Daoist path.'*

*The Daoist-Buddhist Concordance on the Analects* says:
*"One who can regulate this true breath
can settle this true nature.
If the breath is unsettled,
then the heart-nature is unsettled.
If a person can attain this breath
and depart from this breath,
then they may enter the stage of Complete Extinction."*

Tan Zi’s *Book of Transformation* says:
*"The heart is dim and knows nothing,
the spirit is tranquil and wanders nowhere,
the *qi* is serene and does nothing."*

*The Collection of Central Harmony* says:
*"The elixir is refined within the unrefined,
the Dao lies in the realm of non-action.
Regulate the ancestral *qi* by stilling breath and roots—
nurture the infant by forgetting sound and sight.
The practice lies within stillness,
the skill within settledness.
Motionless and silent,
yet responsive to all sensations.
The aged conch holds its pearl,
the silkworm guards its cocoon.
Such is the true mystery beyond measure—
only this: if doubts are shattered,
one suddenly awakens to the True Void.

Within action, one meets the non-action—
the most wondrous paradox lies in the midst of nothingness.
At the moment of vague realization,
within the depths of boundless mystery,
to guard is to delude,
to release is to err.
Neither guarding nor forgetting,
neither restraining nor releasing—
who then holds this existence?
Just so—
await the six Yang phases to be complete,
and embrace the little toad."*

*The Pulse Observations* say:
*"Once the elixir resides in the cauldron,
true fire surrounds it externally,
acting as its protective shield,
constantly maintaining a state of non-thought.
For when the heart is still, the *qi* is harmonious;
when the *qi* is harmonious, the spirit is clear.
Without thought, day after day,
the Great Harmony and the spirit’s *qi* overflow into the golden elixir’s sacred chamber—
parent and child embrace,
and without the encircling power of the spirit-fire,
how could it be retained?
It must not be abandoned for an instant,
night and day without pause—
then naturally the elixir ripens, and the embryo is cast off."*

The Master of Upper Yang said:
*"If the essence is scant, the Returned Elixir will not form.
Great practitioners must know
that their own mercury must always be full—
this is called *'solid abdomen.'*
Once their own mercury is full,
taking the lead is slightly easier—
they must also know
that when gathering the medicine,
the six senses are not present,
the six emotions are all forgotten—
this is called *'empty heart.'*"

*The Compass of the Center* says:
*"If the will is not divided,
then it congeals into the spirit."*

「But when the heart is clarified and all thoughts severed,
the breath is regulated to evenness—
stillness ever radiant,
never let it grow dim or disperse.
Await the *qi* in tranquility,
and the True Person enters *dhyāna* [定].

Within this *dhyāna*,
one perceives the inner landscape—
when the mind’s intent arrives,
the signs begin to stir.
Then one feels a breath arise from the *guī* [规],
murmuring and unbroken,
steadfast and surging,
preserved with sincerity,
heard with the heart—
the six *gāndrā* [根] settled in peace,
the embryo and attendant *qi* [胎扈] congealing,
neither constricted nor counted,
letting it unfold naturally.

When stillness reaches its peak, a sigh emerges—
like fish in spring pools.
When motion peaks, it draws in—
like insects retreating to their shells.
The *yīnyūn* [氤氲] of opening and closing,
its subtleties are boundless.

Thus, after a short while,
one must forget the *qi* and merge with the spirit,
returning to the ultimate unity of *Hún-Dùn* [混沌],
the depths of *emptiness* [虚],
and the steadfastness of *stillness* [守静],
the heart unmoved by thought,
without coming or going,
serene and ever-abiding—
this is called the True Person’s breath with the heels,
the fusion of spirit and *qi*—
this is its sign.

The Master of *Zǐyáng* [紫阳] said:
*"Vague and boundless—
this is the form of *dhyāna* [定]."*

*Dānyáng* [丹阳] said:
*"When the spirit does not stray outward,
the essence and *qi* [精炁] settle naturally."*

Again he said:
*"When the heart is still and thoughts cease,
serene and unmoving—
this is called the True Heart."*

Again he said:
*"Medicinal substances are gathered only when there is no ‘place’ [无里],
the Great Elixir is entirely forged within *dhyāna* [定]."*

*"The Elixir congeals within,
the spirit-fire’s seal enfolds it without."*

I now focus my primordial spirit, congealing and nurturing it within—
naturally the sacred body is perfected,
the ten-month embryo complete,
and the spirit transcends its birth.

This is the Dao of yin and yang,
the source of all transformation and generation.
All life and things arise from it.

Xiao Zixu said:
*"The River Vehicle ferries up to Kunlun’s peak,
not stirring a hair until the Jade Pass is reached—
its marvel lies in the Eight Gates sealed tight,
as yin and yang qi circulates on its own."*

*The Heavenly Immortal’s True Principles* say:
*"After this, the fire stage is called the Great Microcosmic Orbit,
distinct from the prior hundred-day Small Microcosmic Orbit.
Master Lü said:
*'From now on, only blow the windless flute,
from today, strike the stringless zither.'*"

*The Heavenly Immortal’s True Principles* say:
*"The Great Microcosmic Orbit—
like the sun completing one full revolution.
One cycle thus, ten, hundred, thousand, myriad cycles follow.
One moment thus, three thousand six hundred moments likewise—
all to complete the ten-month celestial orbit.
Conception, refining qi and transforming spirit into stillness—
this is the sign of one who has entered.
Within this, some attain stillness in three months,
and thus abstain from worldly flavors.
Some in four or five months, or even longer,
before they cease eating.
The faster one abstains, the sooner stillness is attained.
The slower the abstention, the longer the delay in entering stillness.
For when stillness is achieved, the Original Harmony’s vital qi fills the body—
then hunger is unseen, why eat?
Food is yin; one measure of yin requires one measure of food.
So long as yin remains, one does not transcend.
So long as food is consumed, transcendence is unattained."*

*The Heavenly Immortal’s True Principles* say:
*"A steadfast heart brings easy stillness.
Some attain it in seven months,
some in eight, nine, or ten.
If the heart is scattered, stillness is hard—
some take months beyond ten, even countless,
before achieving it—
this is the result of lingering breath and cold fire,
delaying the Elixir’s power.
Now speaking of those who attain Great Stillness in ten months:
Within this, as the spirit-embryo nears completion,
in the eighth, ninth, or tenth month,
external phenomena abound—
some see wonders, some hear marvels,
some encounter joyous or fearful things,
some trustworthy or deceptive matters,
some arise from delusion,
some are tested by celestial immortals,
or demons come to steal vital qi—
all must be swept away with right mindfulness,
refining qi and transforming spirit with pure intent,
until even breathing ceases and demons retreat."*

*The Heavenly Immortal’s True Principles* say:
*"If a stray thought arises within,
quickly summon right mindfulness—
the stray thought vanishes.
If a demon appears before the eyes,
quickly summon right mindfulness—
do not engage, and the demon retreats.
The *Forty-Nine Chapter Scripture* says:
*'Do not contend with the hemp demon—
those who come will return on their own.'*
Ge Ding Lingyang said:
*'In stillness, deepening the practice,
one may see sages, Buddhas, ghosts, spirits,
palaces, radiance—
do not let the heart cling or reject.'*
Yu Yuwu said:
*'Let a thousand transformations unfold—
the mind unmoved, all evils retreat.'*"

*The Heavenly Immortal’s True Principles* say:
*"Once breathing is truly absent,
qi returns to pure spirit—
no longer is there qi or breath.
If breath remains, though seemingly without leakage,
it is not true cessation.
If breathing is only partially still,
the spirit follows—
only partially still, not fully.
Now is the time for meticulous practice,
entering Great Stillness and pure spirit.
If there is any interruption or separation,
it is like fleeing the Elixir—
one must reach the point of no qi before completion.
This is the second gate’s principle of Returning to One,
restoring the state of primordial union before birth.
A child’s ten months—form complete, life begins.
A spirit-embryo’s ten months—spirit complete, transcendence is achieved.
This is the natural order.
Master Qiu said:
*'If breath is ever unstable by a hair,
life is not yet secured.'*"

*The Heavenly Immortal’s True Principles* say:
*"The Great Microcosmic Orbit’s fire is beyond divination—
not forced, yet not idle,
warmly continuous,
neither clinging to presence nor absence,
initially seeming neither here nor there,
ultimately returning to Great Stillness."*

*The Great Communion Scripture* says:
*"The Dao has no form—
thus within, it is not confined by existence.
True nature is without action—
thus without, the heart is not lost."*

*The Supreme Lord’s Daily Scripture* says:
*"Spirit is the child of qi,
qi is the mother of spirit—
like a hen brooding an egg,
nurturing spirit and preserving qi,
how could they ever separate?
Wonderful! Wonderful!"*

*The Dragon and Tiger Scripture* says:
*"The most subtle essence lies in first having, then forgetting."*

*The Essentials of Nature and Life* say:
*"When the embryo-breath is congealed and refined,
inhalation gathers without accumulation,
exhalation disperses without scattering—
the body’s form becomes void and empty,
merging indistinctly into Stillness."*

Master Qiu Changchun said:
*"A single thought not straying from the mind’s center—this is True Void.
This is the fire of embryo-nurturing,
the True Fire."*

Lu Hongxian said:
*"With each breath, the mind fades into thoughtlessness,
half-awake, faintly sensing the body’s buoyancy."*

Zhang Suqiong said:
*"When refining reaches the point where form and spirit merge in obscurity,
one then knows that color and appearance are True Void."*

*The Hundred-Phrase Chapter* says:
*"Herein lies true faith—
when faith arrives, you shall be astonished.
A single point like a cinnabar orange,
must be met with mercury’s embrace—
no tools or instruments are needed,
for the method inverts heaven and earth."*

Lu Ziyou said:
*"To attain the One is to hold life within oneself—
a body beyond the body,
equal in years to Heaven."*

Shangyangzi said:
*"The Golden Elixir is the primordial *qi* of yin and yang,
the very origin of the Supreme Ultimate,
the root of Heaven and Earth."*

Zhang Ziyang said:
*"All comes down to this single moment’s practice—
eternally preserving boundless ease and joy."*

Shangyangzi said:
*"The Golden Elixir comes from without,
swallowed into the abdomen.
The Returned Elixir—only half a moment—
seizes the creative power of Heaven and Earth,
seizes the creative power of the Supreme Ultimate before division,
seizes the creative power of Heaven and Earth in their copulation,
seizes the creative power of yin and yang’s unfathomable interplay,
seizes the creative power of water and fire’s completion,
seizes the creative power of the Five Phases’ conquests,
seizes the creative power of all things’ genesis—
all gathered in an instant.
How could one not tremble with reverence?"*

Xue Zixian said:
*"The Yang Elixir comes from without,
refining one’s own yin mercury."*

Mei Zhixian said:
*"The yin mud pellet—
a single breath cycles through,
descending through the earthly gate,
ascending to meet the heavenly pass."*

*The Transmission of the Dao Collection* says:
*"When spirit gathers, demons multiply.
Moving true fire to burn the body,
the Three Corpses vanish,
the medicine reaches the sea’s exhaustion—
drawing the River Vehicle’s essence to bathe,
one enters water without ripples.
These are the operations of the River Vehicle."*

*The Transmission of the Dao Collection* says:
*"When the Dragon and Tiger unite and transform into yellow sprouts,
this is the Small River Vehicle.
When the arm’s gold flies and enters the mud pellet,
extracting lead to add mercury to form the great medicine,
this is the Great River Vehicle."*

*The Transmission of the Dao Collection* says:
*"Water and fire embrace,
merging into one,
to enter the Palace of the Spirit."*

「When the breath is settled and inner observation attained,
with a single mind undivided,
both spirit and insight become wondrous.
In stillness, one often hears melodious sounds,
like a dream yet not a dream,
as if amid boundless void,
where winds and landscapes surpass the mundane dust.
Opulence and splendor outshine the human world—
palaces and gates, jade tiles gleaming with frost.
Feathers of jade and brocade, fragrant as clouds of incense,
when this moment arrives,
one ascends the Inner Court,
the yang spirit gathers and returns to the Upper Elixir Field,
refining into an immortal,
to merge with the Great Dao.
A single strike at the Great Gate—
golden light reveals the Dharma Body within the shadowy glow,
amidst flowers in bloom, the mundane form sits still.
Riding the void, one soars across flat plains,
ten thousand miles like stretching one’s arms.»

*The Transmission of the Dao Collection* says:
*"When clouds and thunder descend,
and smoke and flames ascend,
it may be as if the heavens rain strange blossoms,
auspicious winds and celestial qi arise from the palace courtyard.
Or like celestial maidens and jade-feathered cranes,
rainbow-winged phoenixes descending from the Azure Sky,
bearing golden platters of luminous dew and River Vehicle essence,
to present before the Sage.
This is the symbol of the Golden Elixir Returning to the Elixir Field—
the *Ji* (achievement) phase.
The Dragon and Tiger drag the River Vehicle through fire,
surging past the Three Passes,
each pass guarded by countless officials,
their numbers beyond reckoning.
Their armor and weapons strike fear in mortals—
first, the Dragon and Tiger clash yet fail to open it,
then great fire burns until the gate at last unfolds,
until the Kun Chamber cannot contain them,
and they reach the Heavenly Pool before ceasing.
Or like three cranes surging toward the sky,
or twin butterflies entering the Three Palaces,
or five-colored clouds bearing a child in scarlet robes,
passing through the Heavenly Gate,
or golden chariots and jade litters conveying the Sage,
soaring past the Three Realms—
these are the symbols of the *Arm’s Gold Ascending* and the Great River Vehicle.
When one official delivers the decree,
the Nine Continents harmonize in unison,
cycling endlessly, their operations ceasing not—
like wandering the Five Sacred Mountains,
or drifting across the Five Lakes,
or the Celestial Edict commanding the Five Emperors,
or the Sovereign’s mandate summoning the feudal lords—
these are the symbols of the Returning to the Elixir Field.*

*The Transmission of the Dao Collection* says:
*"From above descending below,
the Purple River Vehicle transports essence into the Heavenly Palace,
where wealth and honor abound—
who would not envy?
Coming and going in splendor,
luxury beyond mortal sight,
all present.
Those who follow the Dao
keep themselves pure and serene in daily life,
unbound, solitary, and long withdrawn from the world.
When their practice reaches fulfillment,
their joy knows no limit—
palaces of pearls and jade,
music and dance of celestial maidens,
rare delicacies and exotic feasts,
strange grasses and marvelous flowers,
scenery and breezes like painted visions.
If others do not awaken,
they may think it real—
that one has truly arrived at the Heavenly Palace,
not realizing the Inner Court’s own domain,
mistaking illusion for reality,
and clinging without escape.
Thus, they linger in the dim crossroads,
retain their form in this world,
and fail to transcend their substance to become immortals.

Before reaching the Heavenly Palace,
one remains in inner observation—
outer demons and inner ghosts,
stirred by intent, create false realms,
as if an army of fiends.
Driven mad, they plunge into error,
or lose themselves to heterodox paths,
even failing to become immortals.
For the Three Corpses and Seven Orifices
desire only the death of others,
while their own joy remains unfulfilled.
The Nine Vermin and Six Thieves
torment those who dwell in peace,
leaving no refuge for those who would escape.
Thus, they remain trapped in the world’s illusions,
unable to ascend."*

Zhu Yuanyou said:
*"When the first movement of Yang stirs,
urgently kindle fire to respond—
it must be a fierce boiling and rapid refining,
with the functions of inhalation, licking, and gathering,
forcing the golden elixir from the furnace flames.
Now that the upper opening is achieved,
seize this fiery force,
drive the River Chariot in reverse,
from the tail end against the current,
ascending to Kunlun’s Heavenly Valley Cavity—
like dragons battling tigers,
phoenix waves surging,
shaking heaven and earth.
After copulation,
a single point descends to the Yellow Court’s center.
From then on, apply the function of nurturing warmth—
like a dragon guarding a pearl,
like a hen brooding an egg,
silently returning the light,
neither forgetting nor aiding.
When the Mysterious Pearl takes form,
Taiyi contains the True Essence,
and naturally transforms to transcend."*

Zhu Yuanyou said:
*"When the Golden Elixir forms the embryo,
the pulse halts and the breath stops,
