returning to the chaos of the undifferentiated.
This is the time of my body’s great death.
After long oblivion, rebirth awakens—
one attains the original face,
naturally pure and spotless,
with enlightened nature fully awakened,
the vast earth and sky
transformed into a crystal palace."*

Zhu Yuanyou said:
*"When the Divine Elixir Furnace is established,
guard it with true intent,
protecting it vigilantly—
not a moment may it depart.
If true intent strays from its place,
there may be the danger of confusion and loss."*

Zhu Yuanyou said:
*"The primordial ancestral *qi* is the sovereign,
the post-heavenal essence-*qi* the minister.
Once the furnace obtains the primordial *qi*,
it borrows the post-heavenal essence-*qi*
to nourish and encircle it."*

Yuanzi of the Governing Vessel said:
*"Form and spirit act without effort,
yet essence and *qi* naturally act of their own accord—
just as Heaven and Earth act without effort,
yet all things naturally transform and nurture."*

Master Lü’s *Golden Jade Scripture* says:
*"The dark dragon embraces the One,
the golden pearl radiates supreme light.
The white tiger contains the Three,
the purple snow nurtures the immortal’s bud."*

The *Golden Jade Scripture* says:
*"Nine layers of iron drums sound impartially,
a single golden bell rings upward.
Piercing the Heavenly Hall,
penetrating the Purple Bureau’s Furnace Mountain,
ascending to the Zhurong Peak,
the banks of the Jade Pool—
the *Samādhi* of Threefold Concentration.
A single breath pierces the Yellow Center,
the lead-pearl returns to the treasure vault."*

The *Chant of the True Words* says:
*"Always remain alert and lively."*

The *Chant of the True Words* says:
*"To form the sacred embryo,
first ascend to Perfect Awareness—
this is the essential instruction.
The art of regulation lies in ascent and descent.
The secret of ascent and descent lies in still observation.
Stillness is not absolute stillness—
within stillness, there is movement.
Movement is not true movement—
creation turns in cycles.
Observation is not fixed observation—
within observation, there is awareness.
Awareness is not true awareness—
the numinous light flickers indistinctly.
At this moment,
the furnace is empty yet the elixir is real,
water is firm while fire is yielding.
Each boiling, each refining,
each inhalation, each exhalation—
its essence aligns with Heaven and Earth’s mysterious transformation,
with the sun and moon’s revolutions,
with yin and yang’s purity and turbidity,
with the four seasons’ succession."*

The *Chant of the True Words* says:
*"Refining the elixir is like eating—
too hasty, it burns;
too slow, it rots.
Neither too hasty nor too slow,
then the flavor is complete.
If the elixir’s fire is too fierce,
lead flees and mercury scatters—
thus, it must be gentle, as if barely present.
If the fire is too slow,
the furnace grows cold—
thus, it must be ever-alert.
Neither too fierce nor too slow,
when the moment arrives,
all yin dissipates,
the yang spirit manifests."*

The *Chant of the True Words* says:
*"With a boundless heart,
reaching the sublime where the self is forgotten,
no self, no other—
what heaven, what earth?
Awakening to the empty *qi*,
within the indistinct chaos,
a single point of true yang—
it is me, yet not me;
it is void, yet not void.
Creation turns in cycles,
light and darkness alternate—
divided, it cannot be divided;
united, it cannot be united.
With the yang spirit’s void,
uniting with the Great Void’s void,
they blend seamlessly—
this is the perfection of form and spirit,
uniting with the Dao’s truth."*

The *Chant of the True Words* says:
*"Gentle, as if barely present—
use it without overdoing.
Ever-alert—
guard it without failure."*

The *Chant of the True Words* says:
*"Begin with non-action,
end with non-thought,
then Heaven clears above in serenity,
Earth steadies below in its place,
and only then do yin and yang blend to form the pearl,
collected within the deepest of orifices.
Tumbled, inverted,
dimly luminous—
a single furnace’s creation,
ten thousand measures of divine light."*

The *Chant of the True Words* says:
*"The millet-pearl contains all things,
the four seasons complete,
the eight winds stilled,
the Three Powers fulfilled."*

The *Chant of the True Words* says:
*"Gold’s essence and wood’s fluid clash in battle,
striking the nine-layered *tianluo* bell,
plucking the eight-wind lute—
the sun and moon emerge from the navel,
winds and clouds rise from the armpits,
round and radiant,
yet still a single Clear Void Cavern,
the primordial *hun*’s *qi*—the Supreme Ultimate.
Within it are heaven and earth,
are sun and moon.
Flying, creeping, moving, planting,
egg-born, wet-nurtured—
not a single thing is lacking.
When the numinous spark arrives,
all sounds resound together,
the One Principle manifests—
inexpressible."*

The *Chant of the True Words* says:
*"The *dou* and *gang* stars begin their revolution,
yin and yang invert as a result.
When the work is complete and the Dao achieved,
pure yang’s most potent *qi*
permeates the flesh and refines the bones,
the body’s law is gentle and harmonious,
swallowing all four seasons.
The Great Sun rests atop the head,
with no night.
Creation dwells within the body,
with no killing."*

The *"Chant of the True Words"* says:
*"The qi of the whole body circulates and ascends in cycles,
resonating with the **Great Heavenly Circuit**,
like the flood tide of the fifteenth night—
rising tumultuous and fierce,
penetrating the sinews and purging the marrow,
shattering the bones and joints.
Essential is calmness in action,
clarity in circumstance—
let others unleash winds and waves upon the river,
while my vessel follows the rudder’s turn."*

Zhang Sanfeng’s *"Essentials of the Golden Elixir"* states:
*"The Three Flowers converge at the crown,
the Five Qi bow toward the Primordial.
This is where yin is consumed and yang grows long,
where dross is refined and essence becomes pure.
The whole body is suffused with pure yang—
the old shell is shed, the bones renewed,
the five viscera regenerated,
the hundred limbs re-established.
When the liver is transformed,
its brilliance fills the eyes—
the pupils gleam like tiger’s lacquer.
When the heart is transformed,
its wisdom flows from the mouth—
blood crystallizes into white bones.
When the spleen is transformed,
the flesh solidifies like congealed fat,
the face blooms with powdered radiance.
When the lungs are transformed,
the nostrils scent celestial fragrance,
the complexion returns to that of a child.
When the kidneys are transformed,
the ears hear the music of the heavens,
the hair turns ashen-white with sudden clarity.
With such efficacy achieved,
the spirit naturally departs."*

Zhang Sanfeng in *The Rootless Tree* says:
*"The artisan’s skill is masterful, gripping the helm firm—
let the surging tides churn at the ocean’s depths.
Pass the Three Passes, pierce the Muddy Pill,
and soon the nine orifices of the body are all pierced through."*

Cao Wenyixian, the Immortal Maiden, says:
*"The Original Unity’s internal cultivation alone is true—
seeking breath externally is never complete."*

*The Golden Elixir Key Points* says:
*"Adjust the stepping-breath to be continuous and unbroken,
inhaling and exhaling in harmony—
the mind remains silent, inwardly still and outwardly clear,
as if present yet absent, the spirit condensed, the qi solidified."*

Chen Xiyi says:
*"Sudden—fire wheels seethe the earth’s meridians,
and the spirit bursts forth from the mountain’s peak."*

Qiu Changchun says:
*"The Golden Elixir surges upward, overturning the Heavenly Gang,
what fear of blocked bridges or barricaded passes?
With single-minded resolve, the spirit stirs not—
the six senses unmoved, guiding the circulation."*

*The Records of Daoist-Buddhist Fusion* says:
*"Once the Great Elixir elixir is obtained and the River Chariot is reversed,
entering the Godly Chamber,
if the divine light fails to illuminate,
the elixir loses its counterpart and dissipates swiftly.
Thus, the Original Spirit must serve as the elixir’s refuge,
and the elixir must refine the Original Spirit—
the two abide in inseparable stillness and luminosity."*

*The Records of Daoist-Buddhist Fusion* says:
*"After ingesting the Great Elixir,
the blockages at the Three Passes and Nine Orifices are all cleared.
Know that thereafter, the two *qi* will spontaneously generate,
naturally moving through the now-open pathways."*

*The Records of Daoist-Buddhist Fusion* says:
*"On the Ten-Month Pass and its bodily verifications,
Master Chongxu said:
‘When first entering *dhyāna*, if one steadfastly abides for three months,
the movement of the two *qi* is extremely subtle,
merely stirring at the navel’s void.
If one perseveres to four or five months,
the two *qi*, under the spirit’s stillness and luminosity,
cease their nourishing currents entirely,
all converging at the *dhyāna*-point.
The Original Spirit, nurtured by the two *qi*,
attains unobstructed Yang-Ming and realizes True Emptiness.
The two *qi* cease, the nourishing currents are cut—
only the still-luminous Original Spirit remains as the master of the fetal immortal.

If one guards further to six or seven months,
not only does the mind cease arising and passing,
but even slumber vanishes entirely.
If one guards to eight or nine months,
prolonged stillness and luminosity ensue,
and all meridians still.
If one guards to ten months,
the feet’s yang is pure, the spirit returns to Great Stillness—
thus, stillness generates wisdom,
and naturally arise the *divine eye*, *divine ear*,
*past-life recollection*, *mind-reading*,
and *spirit-realm penetration*.
Earlier, during the refining of essence,
there was already the *leakage-free penetration*;
now, the five later penetrations manifest.

The *divine eye* perceives celestial events,
the *divine ear* hears heavenly speech,
*past-life recollection* reveals karmic causes,
*mind-reading* foretells future matters.
Only *spirit-realm penetration* reveals the spirit’s operations—
if one fails to uphold the Heart-Sovereign,
the spirit-mind will usurp control,
delighting in one’s ability to cultivate and verify,
while the *delight-magic* has already infiltrated the heart.
Thus, one speaks eagerly of worldly calamities and fortunes,
of future schemes—
and disaster follows swiftly.

Only when wisdom is applied without attachment,
and recognition transforms into true insight,
can the fruit of the perfected fetal body be attained.
As the ancients said:
*‘Without interruption for thirty thousand breaths,*
*every step and sit must be clearly aligned with the Dao.’*
This illuminates that the Ten-Month Nurturing of the Fetal Body
lies solely in the unbroken, still-luminous practice.’"*

*The Records of Daoist-Buddhist Fusion* says:
*"If even a thread of drowsiness remains,
residual yin lingers.
If a single perturbing thought arises,
the spirit is not yet pure yang.
One must guard until drowsiness is utterly extinguished,
and all confusion vanishes—
only then is the fetal spirit fully ripe with pure yang.

*The Chaoyang Classic* says:
*‘Three hundred days of fire, ten months of fetal gestation.’*
At this inner stage, clarity dawns—
now, all demons emerge, luring one into other paths.
One must rely on habitual cultivation and virtuous deeds,
and the heavenly spirits will naturally aid.
After the elixir is sealed,
many phenomena arise—
all are the remnants of one’s lifelong habitual thoughts.
At this point, they all manifest.’"*

*The Scripture of the Soul’s Treasure* says:
*"What are called the hundred demons are the six senses, eight consciousnesses, the three souls and seven spirits, the three divisions and eight scenes, and the twenty-four deities within the body."*

*The True Scripture of the Cavernous Mysteries* says:
*"The celestial mechanism suddenly unfurls,
the great earth’s gold shines forth—
the primordial essence’s visage
now reveals its luminous form."*

*The True Scripture of the Cavernous Mysteries* also says:
*"The fleshly eye opens as the wisdom eye,
the common heart, once enlightened, becomes the true heart,
transforming the nature of transformation into the Buddha-nature,
and refining the consciousness-spirit into the primordial spirit."*

**Volume Eight: Detachment from the Fetal Body and Nourishment by Elixir**
*The Mirror of Alchemical Ingredients* says:
*"At the initial fetal formation, observe the native destiny.
At the final detachment from the fetal body, observe the four cardinal directions."*

Master Ziyang said:
*"When the seasonal rhythms have fully turned, the fetal body detaches and the spirit transmutes."*

Old Master Shixian declared:
*"When the elixir ripens, no dragon and tiger remain,
the fire ends, and mercury and lead rest.
Once the fetal body is detached and the spirit transmutes,
one becomes a Celestial Clarity Immortal."*

Ancestor Zhengyang said:
*"The child is young and not yet grown,
it must rely on the nurturing grace of the Mother of the Earth."*

Ancestor Chunyang said:
*"Nine years of fire’s refinement pass directly,
then suddenly, the heavenly gate at the crown bursts open.
The True Person manifests with great magical powers—
from this point, one may be congratulated as a Heavenly Immortal."*

At this time, the *Zhāoyáng Jīng* states:
*"Tend to the infant carefully—whether ten steps, a hundred steps, a thousand, or ten thousand—gradually emerging. Should one be reckless, it will not endure wind and snow. Through long practice until maturity, one penetrates metal and pierces stone, walks on fire and treads water, reaches heaven and traverses earth, comes and goes without hindrance, hidden yet manifest. As one wills, so it is done—whether one or a hundred, a thousand million incarnations."*

The *Huángtíng Jīng* asks:
*"Gazing upon the child seated in stillness,
Who is this child within my own body?"*

The *Cāntóng Qì* commands:
*"Diligently practice without ceasing, day and night.
After three years of hidden nourishment, lightness and boundless movement follow.
Striding through fire, unscathed;
Entering water, unsoaked.
Presence and absence at will—
Endless joy, no sorrow."*

The *Tiānxiān Zhènglǐ* explains:
*"Adjusting the spirit to emerge from the shell as an external body,
From the Upper Field, the mind projects outward;
From the external body, the mind returns to the Upper Field.
With each ebb and flow, the emergence grows refined,
The nourishment deepens.
Thus, after three years of divine suckling,
The spirit becomes complete—
Capable of myriad transformations,
Ascending to heaven and descending to earth,
Crossing seas and moving mountains,
Alleviating drought and flood,
Saving the world and its people,
Destroying evil and banishing harm.
Whatever is wrought is the work of a single spirit.
Spirit transforms, spirit manifests—
This is the Dao of the Immortal."*

The *Tiānxiān Zhènglǐ* further declares:
*"When cultivation reaches the stage of spirit-emergence,
Death and birth are forever transcended.
Calamities and demons hold no sway.
At first, when the spirit emerges—
If it steps out once and returns,
Or twice and returns—
Whether ten steps or a hundred,
One must tend to it with care.
Only then may divine nourishment mature the spirit
Until full ripeness—
Three years hence."*

The *Tiānxiān Zhènglǐ* warns:
*"Adjusting the spirit to emerge from the shell is a critical juncture,
Fraught with great peril.
At first, let it emerge and swiftly return,
Not lingering long,
Nor perceiving distant realms.
With prolonged practice, the emergence may endure,
And distant sights and sounds may be glimpsed before return.
For if it rushes outward too swiftly,
It may lose its true nature."*

Master Zhāng Sānfēng’s *Jīndān Jiéyào* states:
*"Once the infant emerges,
Continuously adjust the spirit,
Endlessly emerging from the shell.
At first, return immediately—
Guard the vital form closely.
From near to far,
The spirit’s heat turns white.
In an instant, a thousand miles traverse.
The elixir furnace and vessel are abandoned—
What further use is there for technique?"*

*The *Chàngdào Zhēnyán* says:*

*"When the Yang-spirit sheds its form,
There is a radiance emanating from the navel wheel,
And a fragrance issuing from nose and mouth—
These are the omens of shedding the form.

After shedding, golden light radiates in all directions,
Hairs and pores glow crystal-clear,
Like the sun rising over the sea,
Or a pearl first glimpsed in the depths,
While the scent pervades the room.

A single thunderous crack—
Golden fire mingles, and the Yang-spirit
Already rests within the *níwán* [cinnabar field, 丹丸].

Once it has emerged,
All depends on one’s daily cultivation.
That is why I first spoke of refining the heart—
This is precisely its purpose.

If the heart is cultivated to be empty and luminous,
Then the Yang-spirit is pure *xiāntiān língqì* [preheaven essence-qi],
Originally devoid of thought or action,
Unstained by encounters, unmoved by sights,
Its retreat and extension under my command,
Its coming and going effortless as ever.
With its entry into the *níwán*,
The body feels as if aflame,
Golden light again streams from the pores,
And the fragrance fills the air once more.

In an instant,
It returns to the *Huángtíng* [Yellow Court],
As though nothing had happened—
Unknowing, unaware—
This is the true realm."*

*The *Chàngdào Zhēnyán* further states:*
*"The Yang-spirit, after shedding its form,
Returns to the Void—
Purple *qì* [vital energy] shimmering within light,
Something yet not a thing,
Form yet not a form,
Symbol-less yet the ultimate symbol,
Soundless yet the source of sound."*

*The *Chàngdào Zhēnyán* declares:*
*"The true Yang-spirit,
After piercing the crown,
Dwells in the *Tàixū* [Great Emptiness],
At ease, unbound—
In an instant, it soars ten thousand miles.

Above, it can caress the sun and moon,
Treading lightly on clouds and mists.
Below, it can roam the islands and seas,
Gazing upon scenic marvels."*

「Thousands of transformations, a will unbound—
All as the heart desires.»

*The *Yánfó Hézōng Yùlù* [Records of the Union of Immortals and Buddhas] states:*
*"When the spirit departs, a scene unfolds—
One must refine the cultivation of nurturing.
Suddenly, within stillness, the Six Radiant [outflows] scatter in the void,
This is the vision of the departing spirit.
Then, one must adjust the spirit to exit the shell,
Stepping beyond the Celestial Gate before withdrawing once more.
To depart is to transcend the Great Emptiness,
To withdraw is to return to the Upper Fields as the place of nurturing.
Know this: the time spent departing and returning is brief,
While the time for nurturing is long.
Departure should not linger—
Even a single step taken must be withdrawn immediately.
With time, one may withdraw after a *lǐ* [~500m], or after many steps,
Or after a hundred *lǐ*, or a thousand *lǐ*—
Yet this must be done gradually, not abruptly.
For if so, the infant-spirit, still young and small,
Might be lost and fail to return.
Or a Heavenly Demon may come to test,
Disrupting the mind—thus one must be cautious in both departure and return,
Only then preserving the entirety of the Void
Amidst the comings and goings,
Lest the great nourishment of the milk-beast [i.e., the primal essence] be lost.

But for those with the seeds of Immortals and Buddhas,
When the initial return-to-the-Void is pure,
The Spirit Platform [mind] is serene and undefiled,
No dust clings—where would dust come from?
This is beyond the reach of ordinary mortals.
Thus, cultivators must prioritize the initial return-to-the-Void as their urgent task."*

*The *Dòngxuán Jīng* [Scripture of the Mystic Cavern] states:*
*"Depart, and roam the world;
Return, and dwell hidden within the *níwán* [mud-ball, i.e., the lower *dantian*].*
Chapter Nine: *Yìngshì Lìgōng* [Responding to the World and Establishing Merit]"

「The Master of the Clouds said: *"To have power without practice is like lacking feet; to have practice without power is to have incomplete vision. When both power and practice are complete, vision is fulfilled. Who says one without power cannot become an Immortal?"*

The Master Lü said: *"The path to Penglai Mountain relies on fulfilling three thousand deeds of virtue, then walking alone in the clouds."*

The Master of Shangyang said: *"When the elixir is refined and the fetal embryo is complete, a child of the Way is born as a True Person, and one must then establish deeds and accumulate merit. Some remain in the world to aid others and guide humanity, like Anqi Sheng and Lan Caihe. Some enter officialdom, rectify the times, and govern affairs, like Dongfang Shuo and Dou Lingjun. As for the Five Ancestors and Seven True Ones, they show boundless compassion and aid others; the Ancestors Zhang, Ge, Xu, Fu, and Qiu ascend upon imperial decree to save the world and assist the Way. If one seeks further advancement, then relocating the embryo and changing the elixir furnace is no great difficulty."*

The Master of Shangyang further said: *"After attaining the Dao, the elixir chamber and its vessels are abandoned. If one does not abandon them, the mind and environment may be defiled, risking dishonor."*

*"The Celestial Master Zhang Daoling, after refining his elixir, told his disciple Wang Chang: 'Taking the elixir should allow one to ascend to the heavens. Yet I have no great deeds to offer the state. How dare I take it so soon? You should first act for the nation’s benefit, removing its calamities, and then take the elixir. Only then can I serve the Three Realms without shame.'"*"

When Sun Zhenren asked the two elders of Yi and Luo: *"I have cultivated the heart for fifty years, yet the heavens do not recognize my efforts. Why?"*
They replied: *"Unless you benefit living beings, how can you ascend to heaven?"*
Thereupon, he returned to Qingcheng Mountain, compiled the *Qianjin Fang* [Thousand-Gold Prescriptions] in thirty volumes, and in broad daylight ascended to the heavens.

*The *Xianchuan Shiyi* [Lost Records of Immortals] states: *"Though practitioners may hide in countless ways, they have not escaped the cycle of death. They must dwell in the subtle realm with their hearts, focus on refining the elixir, establish deeds to aid the outer world, and cultivate their essence to preserve the inner. Only when inner and outer are harmonized can one attain the Dao and achieve lasting existence."*

*The *Qiangyang Jing* [Scripture of the Firewood Grove] says: *"Complete three thousand deeds of virtue, then aid the world and rescue the poor."*

Zhang Sanfeng’s *Jindan Jieyao* [Essentials of the Golden Elixir] states: *"With three thousand deeds fulfilled, the yang spirit transforms and becomes spiritually enlightened, wandering freely through the Eight Extremes without obstruction. It is especially fitting to accumulate deeds and virtue, awaiting the celestial decree to descend, then ascending in broad daylight to the heavens. One attains the highest rank of Heavenly Immortals, equal in magnitude to the Heavenly and Earthly Dao, and radiant as the sun and moon."*

*The *Wuzhen* [Awakening to Reality] says: *"When virtue and power reach eight hundred, and the accumulated deeds of darkness fulfill three thousand, then the balance of self and others, along with the resolution of grievances, aligns with the original vow of Immortals."*

The *Shigan Jidan Zhenghua Ge* [Song of the Stone Chamber Proving the Elixir and Attaining the Dao] states:
*"Hidden in the mortal realm,
Accumulating deeds of virtue in secret.
All who cling to worldly splendor
Shall never reach the Court of Jade Purity.
To the sick, I give medicine;
To the poor, I bestow gold and silver.
I pass on the elixir scriptures to scholars,
And reveal the oral keys to the Way.
When deeds and virtue are complete,
The celestial decree arrives at the Great Polarity."*

*The *Dòngxuán Zhēn Jīng* [Scripture of the Mystic Cavern’s True Essence] says:
*"Conceal your light and withdraw your traces,
Blend with the common and mingle with dust.
Roam within the Three Realms,
Preserve the heart to awaken the world.
Drive away malevolence and support the true Dao,
Manifest forms to enlighten the stubborn and ignorant.
Dispense medicine to cure sickness and suffering,
Scatter wealth to rescue the orphaned and indigent.
Some resolve injustices and punish the wronged,
Others alleviate difficulties and dispel chaos.
They admonish the unfilial and disobedient,
And guide the unrighteous and unvirtuous.
Wherever you go, propagate the great Dao,
Pointing out the path to those lost in delusion according to their karmic inclinations.
Widely bestow the *fǎrǔ* [law’s nourishment],
And guide beings to the Way,
To repay the Master’s virtue,
And to honor the恩 of one’s kin."*"

Chapter Ten: *Tiānyuán Guījí* [Heavenly Origin, Return to the Extremes]」

The **Shàng Yáng Zi** said:
*"When the prenatal essence is fully refined,
And one has already become a True Person,
Then one ascends to the Upper Elixir Field,
Realigns Heaven and Earth,
Renews Yin and Yang,
And gives birth to son and grandson—
A myriad, countless transformations."*

The *Jīn Dān Sìbǎi Zì* states:
*"In one year, a child is born,
Each child able to ride a crane."*

The **Ní Wán Zǔ** declared:
*"In one year, a child is born from the prenatal essence—
Son begets grandson, and grandson branches forth,
Only then is one a true Great Man."*

The **Dān Yáng Zǔ** proclaimed:
*"The spirit fills the boundless void,
Yet meets no obstruction—
Thus, heaven sometimes collapses,
Earth sometimes sinks,
Mountains sometimes crumble,
Seas sometimes dry up.
All formed things eventually decay,
But the Daoist alone remains unshaken through countless eons.
With accumulated virtue, one ascends to the Upper Pure in broad daylight."*

The *Zhuī Yáng Jīng* says:
*"When the second stage of cultivation is complete,
One rescues the world and uplifts the poor.
Refining the eyes to forge the spirit elixir—
The great medicine of perfection—
Form and spirit both attain marvelous purity,
Ascending in daylight,
Whole households lifted to celestial halls.
Yet this depends on the depth of one’s virtue.
If one does not take the spirit elixir,
Only the yang spirit surges upward,
Gazing back at the old corpse—
A heap of dung.
But if one cultivates the great elixir,
The golden pill enters the mouth,
And in daylight, one takes flight—
The universe then shares in its harmony."*

The **Lóng Méi Zi** spoke:
*"After nine years of facing the wall,
The luminous platform is clear,
The sea of awakening is bright,
Form and spirit both attain marvelous purity,
And merge with the True Dao.
Then, nature and life blend as one,
The boundless void becomes the self.
With virtue accumulated to three thousand,
And deeds meriting eight hundred,
One plays among mortals,
Lying dormant, awaiting the moment.
When the Heavenly Scriptures summon,
The body flies to the Golden Gate,
Returning to the Celestial Court—
What worldly wealth can compare?
This is the time when a Great Man fulfills his destiny and achieves renown."*

The *Cāntóng Qì* states:
*"When the Dao is perfected and virtue attained,
One lies dormant, awaiting the moment.
The Great Unity then summons,
And one relocates to the Central Continent.
With virtue complete, one ascends,
Receiving the talismans and scriptures.
The elixir’s efficacy is manifest."*

*"The *Chàngdào Zhēnyán* states:
'To wander beyond the Six Unities in famed mountains,
And observe the winds and *qi* of the eight directions, unmatched.
To pluck the *qin* in the groves of *qí* trees and jade plants,
And cultivate medicines in the halls of jade and fields of *zhī* herbs.
To assist the Celestial Sovereign in the realm of True Dao’s marvelous manifestation,
And hold the pivotal mechanisms in the palace of the Boundless and Supreme Ultimate.
Each attending to their duties without toil,
Each acting in their appointed ways without disorder.
The vastness of Heaven and Earth,
Like fingers upon the palm—near at hand,
What joy could surpass this?'

*The *Chàngdào Zhēnyán* further declares:
'The Dao’s marvel is natural,
The true realm is free and unbound,
Forever free from greed and attachment.'

*The *Chàngdào Zhēnyán* continues:
'Refining a single spark of original spirit,
Like moonlight rippling on water.
Spanning Heaven and Earth,
Permeating the *qiánkūn* [cosmic framework],
All compared to a cluster of violet radiance and golden light—
Ascending to the Three Pure Ones,
Descending through the Six Paths.
One will soon behold the Primordial Celestial Venerable,
And the Ancient Buddha *Pílú Zhēnà*,
Joyfully meeting them,
Shaking hands in fellowship,
After long separation,
Lamenting the delay of this reunion.'

Zhang Sanfeng in *The Essentials of Golden Elixir* says:
'To attain the Heavenly Immortal,
One must face the wall in seclusion.
Choose renowned mountains and blessed lands,
Ancient sites and sacred altars,
Where *qi* gathers and winds are stored,
Build a dwelling beside the clouds,
Backed by shade, facing the sun,
With a dragon’s head suspended like a gem-mirror before you,
And a sacred incense burner standing like a divine blade behind.
With such a supreme setting,
No calamity nor flood can disrupt—
The foundation is secure.
At first, one faces the wall,
Sitting motionless to nurture the spirit,
Emulating the emptied mind guarding the One,
Like a dragon nurturing the pearl beneath its chin,
Or a bird cradling its egg in the nest.
When form and spirit both attain marvelous purity,
And merge with the True Dao,
One enters water and fire without drowning or burning,
And walks with the sun and moon without trace or shadow.'

Cao Wenyixian initially said:
'Nine years of fulfilled labor, the fire’s readiness complete,
Responding to all things without thought—spirit transforms swiftly.'

Shaozi in *Poems of Tranquil Joy* states:
'Only after returning to the banks of the Great,
Do I truly believe a Great Man has been born.'

Zhang Ziyang in the *Preface to the Treatise on Awakening to the True* says:
'To reach this honored title in the Immortal Registers,
And the designation of True Person—
This is the time when a Great Man fulfills his destiny and achieves renown.'

*The *Records of the Unified Dao of Immortals and Buddhas* declare:
'The spirit does not manifest itself;
It returns to the Boundless Ultimate.
The body attains the Void—
Only thus does one perfect their enduring nature.
Heart and *dharma* transform together,
Law is forgotten as one.
Stillness without object,
Illumination without focus.
The Buddha said:
*"To verify the body of the Void,
One must demonstrate the law of the Void.
When the Void is realized,
There is neither ‘this’ nor ‘that’ law."*
The *Chàngdào Zhēnyán* proclaims:
'At this moment, form and spirit both attain marvelous purity,
Violet light and mysterious *qi* fill the heavens and earth.
When manifest, it becomes the sun and moon;
When sharp, it becomes thunder and lightning;
When stirring, it becomes wind;
When nourishing, it becomes rain.
Seeking voices to relieve suffering—
Without sensation, all is communicated.
Holding the pivotal mechanisms of Great Transformation,
One becomes parent to all beings.'

*The *Authentic Scripture of the Cavern of the Mystic Dao* states:
'Entering metal and stone without hindrance or obstruction,
Entering water and fire without drowning or burning.
In concealment, one walks the green mountains without trace or shadow;
In revelation, one fills the *dharma*-realm with myriad forms.
Dispersed, one becomes *qi*;
Gathered, one becomes form.
When form and spirit both attain marvelous purity,
And merge with the True Dao—
A perfect being between Heaven and Earth.
With virtue complete and deeds fulfilled,
Imperial decrees welcome one as guest.
Riding the *zhuànluán* [heavenly dragon] and straddling the crane,
One pays homage to the Celestial Court.
The Nine Mystic and Seven Ancestral lineages,
All attain transcendence—
This time, truly an Immortal,
This time, great renown achieved.
Let the ages pass,
I alone endure forever.

The True Light of the *Dharma*-realm,
Roams freely at will,
Expanding and transforming—
None can fathom its essence.
Revealing the great *dharma* form,
Emitting boundless radiance—
Hundreds, thousands, tens of millions of forms,
Fill the Void-realm entirely.'"
